                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
A Path We Must Eventually Take  
Everyone gets married after being born and growing up. Then they have children, and as those children grow up, they send them off to marry, and eventually, they grow old and die. This is the universal path of human destiny. However, the issue at hand is whether one travels this path well or poorly. This varies greatly from person to person.  
What does it mean to live well?  
The path of life is simple and straightforward. After being born and growing up, one forms a family, has children, raises them, sends them off to marry, and eventually grows old and dies. In this sense, it is simple. However, based on this simple content, whether one travels well or poorly becomes a matter where various complexities arise.  
Everyone wishes to be born and live well. So what is the standard for living well? How does one live well? In ancient primitive times, living in a thatched hut might have been considered living well. But in today's era, that is different. The standards for living well change with the times. Just looking at Korea, today’s wealthy individuals are better off than kings from hundreds of years ago, not even a thousand years ago.  
On November 15, 1969 (Saturday), at the Headquarters Church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
* This speech was given on the last day of the Headquarters District Youth Seminar (November 13-15, 1969).  
8   A Path We Must Eventually Take  
They are within the social system of living well. While there may be differences depending on the era, it is the same for all humans, regardless of gender, that they want to live a little better in their current environment.  
So what is the true standard for living well? What path is a good path to take in life? A woman who forms a family and raises children can be considered an ordinary woman. Living centered around a family is the path that ordinary women generally take. However, when we say someone is doing well, the issue is different. It is not the same as being ordinary. Even being below ordinary is different from being ordinary, but the standards for living well in a way that exceeds ordinary involve various complex factors. To go beyond ordinary standards and seek special criteria, there must be special content involved.  
To walk a special path  
When a woman seeks to walk a path centered on national standards, she must go through trials that are several times greater than those of men. There are many obstacles to overcome. Many difficulties will arise. However, those who try to avoid such difficulties and take an easy path will inevitably face frustration. Regardless of the difficulties, when one does not try to avoid them but rather endures and takes responsibility, those difficulties will bring meaning and determine true value.  
When a person seeks to walk a special path, the materials or conditions that can determine that special content are not what ordinary people desire. That path is difficult, with barriers to overcome and many unwanted circumstances blocking the way. However, one should not try to turn back just because the path is blocked. If it were possible to reach the intended destination that way, then anyone could take that path, and a thousand people would all go that way. Such a path is not one that only special people take.  
Special people do not turn back; they must break through that path. They must go straight and take the shortest route. That is the nature of the problem. To do so, they must overcome trials many times over. There are facts involved that ordinary people cannot imagine. Therefore, unless one becomes someone who can overcome and break through this, they cannot walk that path.  
The same goes for men. Generally, men engage in social activities centered around issues like educating their children or economic matters. In other words, most people usually focus on family-centered activities. The ordinary path for a man is an easy one. However, for those who aspire to do exceptionally well, there are myriad difficulties.  
From this perspective, for a man in South Korea to take the best path, he must choose a path that represents 15 million men, half of the 30 million population, which is the one path that all 15 million dislike. Without doing so, he cannot walk the path that represents all 15 million. A man who says he will represent all 15 million must take responsibility for the path that all 15 million would retreat from and break through. Only then can he occupy a position where he can be said to have done well as a man.  
The standard of true success  
Today, many men claim to have succeeded through social activities, but what is the standard of that success? No matter how successful one may be, if that success is for their own family and children, it does not represent the nation or the 30 million people. That is the reality.  
For example, if the President of South Korea leads the nation while moving based on his family, he should be criticized by the 30 million citizens of this country. He must work, move, and struggle based on a national perspective that goes beyond his family; otherwise, he will be criticized by the nation.  
10   A Path We Must Eventually Take  
However, if he moves based on the hope that all 30 million people would follow that national foundation, he will be remembered in history as a leader of the nation whom the people can revere. That foundation should not be centered around his own children and family.  
When a woman seeks to walk a special path, she should not base it on a common family environment. If she does not possess an overall content that allows her to live centered on a national foundation, she cannot walk a special path. In other words, one cannot walk a path centered on both family and nation. To be a special person, one must have a national standard.  
Next, when expanding the scope to a global level, what should one do? In a world of 3 billion people, one must walk a special path representing all of them. Since it is a path one takes with their life at stake, and many people have come and gone throughout the thousands of years of history leading to today’s 3 billion people, to become a figure who will be remembered in history as a representative of all those people, one must not walk the same path that others have walked. If it is a path that anyone could think of, hope for, or walk, many people would have already taken it. Therefore, when one decides to truly walk a path that is genuine and special, a model path that no one has walked before, they must conclude that they need to go beyond the current 3 billion people and aim for a higher position.  
So how should you walk that path? There will be strong walls blocking the way that have never existed in history, and there will be difficulties that society has not resolved thus far blocking the way. What should you do then? You must not retreat from that position. That would be of no use. No matter how much you have run tirelessly for ten years, if you cannot achieve your goal, you may avoid criticism but will leave no standard to be praised. This is a serious issue.  
So where should you start your journey? If the people of South Korea say they are going out for the world based on the national ideology of South Korea, that is nonsense. When you say you are going for the world, you must go with the world as the stage. You cannot go out without a global foundation. At the same time, you cannot say you will go for the world, for South Korea, and for your family all at once. There cannot be three foundations simultaneously.  
The path we must inevitably take  
In the grand scheme of things, the small is always included. That is, individuals, families, nations, and countries are all included in the world. From this perspective, what is the center of the individual? It is the family. The center of the family is the nation, and the center of the nation is the world. However, humans cannot go all at once while wanting to go all at once. If a person is destined to eat once and die, they would rather eat in front of the world than eat and die in front of just individuals. Similarly, life is only once. One cannot go once and say they do not want to return. Once gone, that is the end.  
Therefore, you have an inevitable path in life that you must take. How should you go? Most people live their lives centered around their families, coming and going until they die, and such people are no different from those who have come and fallen like leaves throughout history.  
The Unification Church may seem to be centered around families globally today, but that center is not the family. If the Unification Church were only centered on families, it would have no relation to God. It would deviate from God's direction. Wouldn't it? The Unification Church is centered on the world. No matter how capable one is or how much they live for their country, if they do not align with the central standards of the world, their efforts for the nation will also fall like leaves.  
12   A Path We Must Eventually Take  
Historically significant figures such as great people, saints, or presidents are those who have lived their lives in alignment with the center of the world along with heavenly fortune. They have lived beyond their own nations, with content that future generations can commemorate thousands of years later, living for the world and all humanity.  
Such people have walked their paths even when opposed by their nations, ethnicities, or families. For them, such opposition is not an issue. They continue on even when opposed by the entire nation under the sovereignty of the state. So who remains in the end? What foundation did such people start from? It is centered on the world. They will pursue that. Thus, even if families, tribes, nations, and countries disappear with the times, those who have pursued ideals from that perspective will surely move history forward.  
So what will they do by moving history? They will seek a way to connect the world. Therefore, the starting point of the journey is always a problem.  
You are young people. You will eventually get married, have children, and live. But what should you center your life around? Will you start anew centered on your family as a member of one family among 30 million people, or will you lead your family and start centered on this nation and ethnicity, or will you start from a foundation that transcends the nation and the world? What will you choose? This is the issue.  
What do you want to choose? Please answer. "It is the path to the world." It is easy to say. The problem arises here.  
Everyone wants to become great and excellent; there is no one who does not. But why can’t they? It is because the starting point is wrong. Therefore, you must establish the correct starting point. Can you go for the world just by shouting loudly within South Korea? You cannot.  
That is why humanity needs a new awareness and ideology, a new principle. This ideology should be such that when it is proclaimed, people with a good conscience around the world can see it and say, "Yes."  
Even if there are opposing countries, you must break through. Even if it means risking your life, you must go. Even if there are environmental obstacles in front of the path, you must not succumb to those obstacles. You must go with the conviction to step over them. If you do so, even if your body may be conquered, your conviction and ideology will not be conquered. Ultimately, those who conquered will be conquered in turn by those who were conquered. God works in such a way. Ultimately, what started from a difficult position will pass. Therefore, we young people must walk this inevitable path of destiny.  
The issue is where to start  
So the question is, where should you start your journey? Will you live with a fixed mindset on something? If you were born as Kim, will you live lamenting or rejoicing in the position of being Kim's child? Or will you hold onto the nation and the people, lamenting and rejoicing together? Further, will you hold onto the world even if it means dying, or will you live holding onto the world? This is the issue. Based on this standard, myriad situations arise.  
Those who pursue such a supreme standard are vertical figures. There is only one vertical path. Being vertical means being connected to God. This is the standard you must establish for yourself. Being vertical means ascending to one place.  
When women get married, some may think, "I was born a woman, so I will find a man," while others may think, "I am getting married to save the nation." However, a woman getting married...
Going to get married is not to share joy with a man. It is not to meet a man. It is not for the happiness of a family or a woman. If one says they are going to get married on behalf of all women in the Republic of Korea, to marry for this country, then that person is a great individual. Do you understand what I mean?

Looking at our country, there have been instances in the past. There is a woman named Masako (方子), who became the wife of Prince Yeongchin; she came from Japan to Korea. Why did she come? Did she come because she loved a Korean man? No, she came for the country. Such individuals remain in history. After the annexation of Korea by Japan, she entered into a political marriage to establish some relationship. That woman will remain in history as a representative sacrifice of all Japanese women. Is that correct or not? Then, marriage is the same for everyone, so why does only that remain in history? Because the value is different.

So, who in the entire world tried to marry from the highest position? It was Jesus. When Jesus came to receive his bride as a groom, from what position did he come? He came for the world. Who is the representative figure that came to marry for the world? There is no one but Jesus.

Until now, there have been women who married for the country, but there has never been a man who married for the country. When a man marries, he completely loses himself, right? (Laughter) However, there has been a representative in history who said he would marry for the sake of the world, and who is that? It is Jesus. Then, in terms of the content of marriage, is it fundamentally different? It is the same as taking one woman as one man, and it is the same to marry and have children. There is nothing different; it is the same.

However, to say that one will marry for the world is different. Marrying for the world is beyond marrying for the country. When one marries for the world and establishes a global family, that family stands in a position greater than a national family, or represents more than a national family; it stands as a family that represents all families.

Then, who is the one that comes as the owner of the most victorious family, hoping for the most victorious family? It is the Lord of the Second Advent, as spoken of in Christianity. To marry, one must do so splendidly. From that perspective, the Unification Church makes good discoveries. Then, if we were to name that person, what name would we give? The most appropriate name to call that person is "True Parents," as designated by Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. How is it? Is it a good name? This is a simple and straightforward term, but when you understand its meaning, it is a great term.

Then, where is the point of their life? It is not centered on the family. The point of fluctuation is centered on heaven and earth. There is no place that person goes that is not heaven and earth. There is no historical act that is not historical. Every action of that person will remain forever with a value more precious than anything in history, from one to ten million things. Even a scrap of paper that person used will remain as a historical legacy. Everything is global; it cannot be anything but universal. A great person does not become great because their lineage is different. A person who is determined to go this path, even if it means sacrificing their life to save the world, is a great person. If they cannot go in their own generation, they will go through the second, third, or tenth generations; that person is a great person. Heavenly fortune cannot help but move through people. It is like a compass that is automatically drawn to a large, strong piece of iron beside it, even if the compass stays still.

When you look at your ancestors, what kind of good ancestors are they? Are they good ancestors who lived only knowing their own children, their own wives, their own husbands, and their own parents? No. Good ancestors are those who, even at the cost of their own families, sacrificed for their neighborhood, centered on that neighborhood for their township, centered on that township for their county, and centered on that county for their nation and people. Where are the young ladies here? Answer me. Is that right or not?

However, these days, young ladies often cry and make a fuss, saying they promised to love someone and then abandoned them. Moreover, women cling to men, saying, "If it’s not you, I will die." But those trivial matters, if they die, the country will not perish. 

So, you must become people for whom if you die, the country will inevitably perish. You must be a family that can hear that if you die, the country will perish, and if your family perishes, the families of thirty million people will perish. Therefore, even if thirty million people die, your family must remain. To do that, what must you do? You must achieve victory through hardships that thirty million people have not experienced. That is how it must be.

Jesus also tried to establish a foundation centered on the world, so even when the fate of the cross was approaching, he prayed through the night, saying, "Abba, Father, everything is possible for you. Take this cup from me. Yet not what I will, but what you will." (Mark 14:36) My will is close to my own blood relatives and the people of Israel, but when viewed through your high and broad will, it is like the doomed Gentiles.

Just as you are willing to sacrifice yourself for those who are unrelated to you, your heart is different from my will, but I will completely set aside my will and obey your will to save a broader world. Because he died with that heart, the history of the world remained centered on God's providence, and because of that, Christianity could not help but become a global religion. That is how it happened.

Then, does the Unification Church have a path to follow? Just as you as individuals have a path to follow, and the Republic of Korea has a path to follow, does the Unification Church have a path to follow? If so, what kind of path is it? In walking that path, will there be instances where men die and women die? You must not think there won't be. Behind a nation that lives and prospers, there are tragedies that you cannot even imagine swirling and following one after another. Even in our Republic of Korea, you must understand that there are people dying in the North, or on the front lines or overseas, to save this nation.

In this view, the destiny of this country is not sustained by anyone but by those people. Because of their efforts to endure and overcome everything to establish a heavenly foundation, the path of the Republic of Korea remains, and the foundation for the happiness of this country is laid, and the path of destiny is opened.

What kind of path does the Unification Church have to follow? Among the paths that Jesus wanted to take and the path that the Unification Church wants to take today, which is the greater path? You all tell me. Which is greater? "The Unification Church." Is it really greater? "Yes." What is greater? Is it the size of the head, the size of the body, or the amount of food eaten? They are all the same. But what is it that is greater? It is the greatness of thought. It is the greatness of thought and determination. To swallow the world, one must surpass the thoughts of the world. One must make a determination greater than that of the people of the world. When united in that way, the power of that unity, even if it is a small group, will not be dismantled for a thousand years, even if compared to the unity of three billion people in the world. However, the power of the world will be dismantled in a hundred years. If a small number unites with a power that will not be dismantled for a thousand years, that power will swallow the world and still remain.

Then, what is the principle that the Unification Church advocates? "It is the principle of the Heavenly Sovereignty." Then, what does the term "Heavenly Sovereignty" mean? The term "sovereignty" (宙) means "house." A person must enter and exit based on their house. There are parents, children, siblings, and relatives; one must enter and exit centered on that foundation. This is the normal path of life.

However, the question is whether the foundation of this path is centered on oneself, on the nation, on the state, on the world, or on the Heavenly Sovereignty. Which is greater, cosmopolitanism or heavenly sovereignty? "Heavenly sovereignty." That sounds good. The words are nice. Right now, you are in the process of entering into heavenly sovereignty. Is that correct? "Yes." 

Then you will become a prosperous lineage. How prosperous will you be? Most young women might say, "When I come to Seoul, I will wear one beautiful skirt, but when I succeed and go back, I want to wear twelve skirts." And when a girl from the village says she is going to Seoul, if you ask her what she will do there, she will say she will marry a good husband if she finds one. However, while marrying an ordinary person is not particularly difficult, finding a husband who can go in and out for the sake of the world is extremely difficult. If such a husband is found, it is not about twelve skirts; it will be a skirt that can fan out towards the world.

Women want to come to Seoul at least once in their lives. So, they always have unrealistic thoughts. They dream even while eating. No matter how much they eat millet or barley rice now, will they live only on millet and barley rice forever? When will they fulfill that wish? They must make their own determination. They must think about what kind of man they want to take as their husband. However, just making plans and standing on the street does not mean that person will become their husband.

So, what must they do? They must catch that person's eye. To catch their eye, they must be higher than that person’s gaze. However, men also want to marry women who are better than themselves. That is the nature of men's desires. It is probably the same for the disabled. Isn't that right? If you ask anyone, you will get the same answer. Every man wants to marry a woman who is better than himself.

Women are the same. Do women want to marry better men or worse men? Let’s hear an honest answer. Women may not answer, but deep down, they want to marry the best man. Women, give me an answer. Do you want to marry a good man or a bad man? "……." This is the problem. This is why it can only be said that men are slightly better than women. They may have answered ten times in their hearts, but they cannot bring themselves to say it out loud. (Laughter)

But just wait and see. In the future, when there is a handsome man of unparalleled beauty in front of them, and someone asks, "Who wants to marry him?" the person who firmly decides and raises their hand first will end up marrying him. That time may come. So, practicing answering is also good. It is possible.

Sometimes, do you have moments like this? You might toss a coin to see if you have good luck or bad luck. If the coin lands on heads, you feel good and go on your way, but if it lands on tails, you feel bad and might even turn back. It affects your mood. So, when tossing the coin, you wish, "Let it be heads, let it be heads, please don’t let it be tails." Do you pray like that? If there is a serious issue of life and death hanging in the balance, will your eyes widen or not? Will your hands tremble or not?

Depending on how things unfold here, heaven and hell are at stake. Since you are still in your twenties, you may not be thinking about marriage, but try becoming a single woman over fifty. You would want to marry even an old man. In any case, it is certain that everyone wants to find a good man, right? "Yes."

Then, can you do that as you please? Can you do it as you wish? It does not happen as you wish. If you are longing for the son of a nobleman, thinking, "That son will wash his face in the morning and sleep at night. Right now, he is eating," and you think about him all day, can he become your husband? Just because you think about him all day does not mean he will become your husband. It does not work that way. To accept him as your husband, you must first catch his eye. To catch his eye, you must be able to accompany him on his path, and when he goes astray, you must be able to give him a nudge to correct him and lead him to a good path. When you are that kind of woman, even if you stay quietly at home, he will hear rumors and come looking for you.

To become the bride of Jesus

Jesus could not live openly. He lived in hiding. When he was born in Bethlehem, he was born alone, not knowing whether he had a father or not, whether he was a legitimate child or not, and he was born in loneliness. After being born, he had to flee because they tried to kill him. After spending about three years in that state, he wandered around the shores of Galilee. Even while in Jerusalem, he could not show his face.

However, there was something within him. That became a rumor. How much of a rumor was it? It became a global rumor. How much has the rumor spread today that Jesus has come as the Lord who is the groom? It has spread globally through Christianity. That is why Christians have fought until now, saying they want to take him as their groom. But did they take him as their groom or not? "They could not."

Everyone, how wonderful would it be if I could become his bride? Have you thought about that? How wonderful would it be? Would it be as good as eating a full meal of bulgogi? Would it be as good as when people from the countryside go to a Chinese restaurant and eat to their heart's content? Such bulgogi or Chinese food cannot be compared.

So, when Jesus came to this earth, who should go to find him? Should the groom come to find the bride, or should the bride go to find the groom? The bride should go. Is it because the groom is an unworthy man or a worthy man? It is because he is worthy. Hearing the rumor of his worthiness, countless people from around the world are earnestly trying to meet the groom, Jesus, day and night, whether it is morning or evening.

However, because he is a great person, he cannot be met in a trivial way. He is the prince of heaven advocating the tremendous principle of heavenly sovereignty that transcends the world. But if you pray with the mindset that you are a woman from the Republic of Korea and that you must wear a hanbok when he comes to the wedding, will that groom appear? That groom is a global person, so to become a bride who can welcome that groom, you must be greater than that groom.
You must have a sense of humor. But when a woman who is to be a bride asks Jesus, "How much do you love me? To love me, you should love me like this. Why do you do that? Are you the renowned bridegroom of the world? And you should love God like this, what does that mean?" If she were to say such things, how would the bridegroom feel? Would he feel good or bad? Would a bridegroom want a bride who speaks like that? (Laughter) Don't laugh too much. The teacher is speaking lightly now, but this is a serious issue. When the teacher talks late into the night, if you are dozing off, it makes him feel bad and he won't want to talk. You need to at least put on a smile on your stiff faces so that he feels like speaking.

If you look closely, most Korean women are expressionless and stiff like bamboo, lacking charm. There’s nothing to see. A woman should laugh for at least three hours a day. It’s necessary before getting married. Even if it’s just dancing a little, she should be able to laugh to be a well-rounded person. But don’t use the teacher as an excuse to avoid practice, okay? If parents see that, they will think you are crazy.

Anyway, if there is such a bride, and she asks Jesus, "What are you? What is the way of the cross? If you can do anything, why not do it like a man... not according to my will, but according to your will... What is that trivial thing?" How would the bridegroom, the prince of the lower world, feel? Think about it, men, how would you feel? "It feels bad." But while feeling bad and angry, wouldn't you also think, "Wow, that’s really cool"? 

Also, wouldn't you think, "How great it would have been if you had become my disciple 2,000 years ago"? Would you think that? Even if you are a woman, wouldn't you think how great it would have been if there had been a disciple like you back then? And if Jesus has a desire for him to be a disciple, wouldn’t he also think, "I hope you become my bride"? "Yes." But what makes you feel bad? (Laughter) Why do you feel bad?

If there is such a woman, could it be said that God would not want her to complain before Him, the Lord of Christianity who has built up merit for thousands of years as a prince of heaven? It cannot be said. If a woman were to come out and protest, "What have you done as a man born into this world? You are saying you are the bridegroom? What have you done without getting married even after turning 30?" How would Jesus feel? He might outwardly feel bad, but inwardly he would be dancing with joy. I think so, but what about you? Would you dance or feel bad? Outwardly you might feel bad, but inwardly you would be filled with hope. And don’t think that the teacher is forcing you to say that. It is the truth. Right? "Yes." Still, men do have some potential. Think about it.

Our starting point
You who have entered the Unification Church must not be inferior to Jesus. The Unification Church is a high standard, so you must live even more splendidly than Jesus. That is why the teacher speaks informally to Jesus. 

Why die like a foolish person? 
If the teacher says this, would Jesus feel bad? If there was a way not to die, Jesus would say, "I didn’t know there was such a way until now..." Then he would think, "If I had done this, I wouldn’t have had to die, and I could have fulfilled my purpose..." and would be grateful when the teacher teaches him. Originally, Jesus was meant not to die. If you teach Jesus this, would he feel bad and think, "You have taken my place, you enemy," and draw a sword? No, that is not the case.

The founder of the Unification Church does not die so easily. If mainstream church members hear such words, they would feel bad. Would they just feel bad? Their hearts would drop. Not just drop, but they would feel completely crushed. So you need to know which words are more practical.

So what has come out of this? What is it called? It is called the Principle of Heaven. The Principle of Heaven is the house of God. Since it is God’s house, can God enter or not? "He can enter." If God enters, can this world enter or not? "It can enter." Then can Jesus enter or not? A hundred people can enter and still have room left. You need to understand that. 

The Lord (주) is the house. This Principle of Heaven is our starting point. Therefore, even when taking a single spoonful of rice, it is for the world, and seeing things is also for the world. However, if it goes against that, it is all negative. My hands may not have welcomed spring yet, but when the day comes to welcome spring, I will not let such things go.

That doesn’t mean I will cut their necks.
You must be different from them. Your way of seeing should be different, your ears should be different, your sense of smell should be different, and your speech should be different. Although we live in the same world, we must be different.

What kind of warriors are we? We are warriors of unification. Is unification something pleasant or unpleasant? "Pleasant." Really? Doesn’t the word unification make you feel nauseous? Just hearing the word unification makes me feel nauseous. Because of the name unification, I have more wrinkles. Do people in South Korea like unification? They like the unification of North and South Korea, but who would like the unification of the Unification Church? Only you who are here might like it. But whether you truly like it or not is something to be tested. You have to sift through it to know. When you sift, the dregs will all come out. There are dregs in everything. There are dregs in diamonds and in gold. Among the thirty million people of South Korea, there are many dregs.

When we receive that power surrounding us, it brings infinite strength, and when we absorb that power, it gives us new shocks and stimulations as eternal strength. We must become sons and daughters who can experience the existence of the Father, who is always close, who gives life and fills us. We must realize how precious it is to grow as your children in such a place and how valuable it is to be able to discuss the journey of life with you.

Many people on this earth are hoping for heavenly fortune or the dawn of their own lives, but we know that they are hoping from a relative distance. However, we must clearly understand that, unlike them, all authority in life and the center of life begins from you, the Father, and all glory begins from you, the Father, who is the center of admiration. 

To do this, we must realize that you are deeply with us in our hearts and close to us, governing all our affairs, becoming the driving force of our lives and the source of all our emotions. We must understand how precious it is to be able to host you, who is wide, deep, high, precious, and of infinite value, and that when we prove that standard a million or even a billion times, we establish the authority to govern the universe and absorb all the contents of heaven.

We must clearly understand that when we are led by our desires and captured by external conditions, losing ourselves, and when we are caught up in bodily desires and become people of external desires, we are placed at a distance from ourselves and the Father.

We want to walk together with you, Father, so we must learn to hear the cries of life that penetrate deeply into our hearts, to hear the voice of the Father walking the path of restoration, and to be sons and daughters who can hear the new commands that you issue from the depths of your heart.

This morning, the reason we have gathered here is to hear your voice, to hear your counsel, and to find the new path of destiny you present. Please remember our anxious appearances. Please remember our lonely appearances. Please remember our infinitely sorrowful appearances, Father, in your heart.

When your compassionate heart wells up from within us, and when we keep this day to fulfill what you desire, and when the heart of admiration wanting to cross the line of death with you ignites, we can seek you, the source of life, and we believe that you are prepared with all your almighty power. Therefore, we must become your children who can feel your heart and sanctify it with love.

Especially at this time, it is a historically holy time. Like the heart of a beautiful girl waiting for the light of life in the world of darkness, like the heart of a shepherd burning with hope, waiting for the morning, we prepare secretly from dawn to meet a day with you.
Thinking about how much the Father would cherish this moment, I earnestly hope and wish that You would allow us, the gathered brothers, to come before You and praise You with our precious, high, and infinite value.

Though we call upon You with our feeble voices, it is not for our own happiness, but to save our nation and the world that we cry out. We must understand that when we call out with such a heart, You are surely present before us and within us. Even if we are lacking in strength, when we strive to fulfill Your wishes and ask for strength before You, allow us to know that the power moving within Your bones is with us.

Let us, in our lonely places, pour our hearts into resolving the sorrows of our nation, the world, and the universe. We also wish to raise our hands to block those who are rushing toward death under the evil powers, wanting to forget their pride and face in order to save them, and we wish to struggle and lament our weakness while training our strength. In the places where we cry out to become such selves, we know that You are always helping us. For this reason, those who walk the heavenly path are not comfortable people.

This body seeks strength, but it also has infinite weaknesses. That is why Jesus said to be like this on earth. When we look at our parents, they are the embodiment of the wishes of the whole, the symbol of longing, and the source of happiness. They are the motive, the process, and the result. When we think of the relationship between parents and children, the motive is the Father, the process is the Father, and the result is the Father. We must understand that there is a heart of the Father that can embrace us in that holy place where we long to see the Father, desire the Father, miss the Father's will, take the Father as the source of love, and establish a relationship of harmony with the Father.

Thus, we must know how much the Father has longed for sons and daughters who penetrate the Father's heart, longing for the embrace of the Father. The children receive the life’s sustenance of the Father and Mother, inherit the heart and desire of the Father and Mother, and can look toward the future through the children. We must understand that this is the place where the relationship of the wealthy Father is established, and we must pursue that holy place.

As we truly call upon the Father, not letting go of the Father we miss, placing my cheek against the Father's cheek, and repenting in the unity of the Father's tears and the son's tears, who can stop the footsteps of sacrifice that are going forth to find one world? Even Satan must submit here, and it is the original principle of creation that Satan must participate in this place, so allow us to be sons and daughters who can be like that.

We must not have hearts like the cold, harsh winds of winter. There must be a day like the spring sun that comes into our hearts, like the month of March, filled with warmth.

Moreover, this heart must spread wide toward the Father, receiving a ray of light that brings the dead life back to life, blooming anew, releasing fragrance, inviting butterflies, and creating a garden of joy that can harmonize with heaven and earth through ourselves. Thus, we must know how much the Father has longed for the appearance of sons and daughters who can live joyfully in the embrace of the Father.

We ourselves must also be able to be embraced by the Father, wipe away our tears, receive the support of joy, and be able to be called the sons of the Father. We must become sons and daughters who understand that this joy is of infinite value that cannot be compared to anything in the world. If there are such sons and daughters, how could we forget the Father, how could we sin against the Father, and how could we escape from the Father's dominion? I earnestly hope and wish that we may become sons and daughters who clearly understand this fact.

Father, the year 1969 is coming to an end. We must once again step over the understanding that remains for us in these 40 days.

Father, we must understand once more what Your wishes are for us and start anew. As we welcome the new 1970s, let us long for the holy appearance that can praise the Father with a harmonious countenance, having passed through the tedious winter season of the past days and welcoming the spring season. Allow us to be Your sons and daughters who can resolve to become such a figure, to be the new workers of the Father.

This morning, I once again bring this before the Father. Please give strength to the children of unification. Have we grown weary while following the Father’s will? The Father has not grown weary. Have we thought of ourselves while following the will? The Father has never thought of Himself.

Father! You are the subject, and we are the object. Although the subject and object should become one, we should not be so far apart. This is entirely our fault, our inadequacy, and because we are in the realm of sin, we must realize this. While praising the holiness and victory of the Father, allow us to be Your children who can keep pace with the Father and accompany Him.

Please allow us to be sons and daughters who can be embraced in Your bosom and find eternal rest. Father, I earnestly ask and wish that You would allow many sons and daughters whom You can be proud of through the Unification Church.

There are numerous denominations and countries in the world. There are also thirty million living in the Republic of Korea. However, depending on how many children can be remembered before the Father in such a place and embraced in the Father’s bosom to be loved, the fate of the world can be determined, and the fate of that nation can be determined. Allow us to understand that we have a historical and heavenly mission to comfort the Father in such a place. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Today, I will speak on the topic of "Betrayers and Heaven."

Judgment of Good and Bad in General Society and the World of Faith
In our daily lives, the concept of good and bad exists for everyone. What I consider good can be thought of differently from various perspectives.

Depending on the type of business, there are good and bad aspects in promoting that business, and even when centered around a nation, there can be good and bad aspects.

Moreover, in external relations centered around the existence of the nation, there will be countless variations. This includes the world of nations. Externally, there can be good and bad aspects in the relative world centered around the nation, and conversely, from a subjective standpoint, there can also be good and bad aspects when looking at one’s own conscience.

In the relative world, the good and bad are often determined by the results identified through some process. Whatever business one undertakes, one hopes for good at the beginning, but we often see that the results turn out poorly.

In your personal life, when you start the day with certain tasks or purposes, if everything that happens throughout the day does not go as intended, we inevitably feel that it is bad. Thus, the results that appear become the axis that determines good and bad.

Next, when we think about our conscience, it is the same. You may feel this a lot. Those who engage in special faith practices or pursue spiritual lives feel this immediately. When encountering someone for the first time, one can sense whether that person is good or bad without a process. This means that when dealing with a person, if one focuses on conscience, one can feel it without going through a process. Even in the first encounter, one can discern the results of good and bad. Many of you may have experienced this in your faith life. Those who have had spiritual experiences have this.

Thus, the quickest way to determine good and bad is in interpersonal relationships. Good and bad are quickly judged among people.

However, the results of good and evil are not necessarily determined by some nature or external worldly matters. It is determined by the heart in the relationship between people. However, general society decides good and bad based on external rather than internal, from the perspective of the object rather than the subject. This means that good and bad are determined based on the results that appear after going through a process. Of course, even those who have had spiritual experiences cannot foresee the results. They do not have such serious and responsible relationships.

The Highest Standard Pursued by Humanity
Humans must have both internal and external relationships. The internal relationship is the relationship with other humans, while the external relationship is the relationship with the world. This is the relationship that people have.

Why is this? It is because humans are beings of reason and nature. According to our principle of creation, humans have relationships with the external world, that is, how to relate to the world of all things, how to relate to nations, and internal relationships, that is, relationships with other humans. These two directions are different. Therefore, we come to know that there are external and internal relationships when deciding the issue of good and bad.

Then, what is an enemy, and how does it arise? An enemy is something that obstructs one’s wishes and completely destroys what one is determined to accomplish. This is true in both external and internal relationships.

As beings created in the image of God, who is a being of reason and nature, we ourselves possess both introspective and outward characteristics. In other words, we exist in a reciprocal relationship between the introspective and the outward.

However, what do all people long for? They long for personhood. They also hope to succeed. They desire success. However, just because a person has succeeded does not mean that their heart has particularly broadened. It does not necessarily grow larger. Their power may grow, or their environment of glory may expand, or they may become the richest person in Korea, but that does not mean that their heart has grown larger. The heart itself does not grow. It may have grown, but what has grown? It has only grown outwardly; fundamentally, that person has not grown.

So, what does our individual self pursue? It pursues personhood. What is the highest standard of that personhood? It is centered around conscience and is based on the highest peak. Then, what is the highest peak of conscience? Conscience must pursue goodness, and the highest subjective being pursuing that goodness is the ideal being with a personality, which leads to the concept of God.

From the standpoint of pursuing personhood, as one ascends toward that highest standard, one cannot be satisfied with just humanity or personhood. One cannot be satisfied with the emotions that come from flat relationships in everyday life. Satisfaction is found in a three-dimensional world, not a flat one. When stimulated by the three-dimensional world that seeks the highest peak centered on personhood, one feels happiness there.

Happiness comes from the combination of personal content that transcends life. Therefore, the highest standard that humans pursue in seeking personhood is not a flat standard. It transcends to seek personhood from a three-dimensional standard, which is how concepts like philosophy and religion came into being.

Thus, the question of the existence of God arises. The history that humanity has walked cannot be denied, and we must understand that humans are standing on a path of fate that cannot deny God. In this way, we humans are pursuing the highest standard. Next, we pursue ideals. So, where is the peak and end of pursuing that ideal? It is the pursuit of one world. Ultimately, the highest standard that humanity pursues is God.

The Point of Division Between Betrayers and Victors
Here, the concept of God emerges. Humanity has pursued God. Over six thousand years of history, humanity has not distanced itself from God but has approached Him. Here, one must be a plus (+) and the other a minus (-). Plus cannot meet plus. Neither can minus meet minus. There must be a relationship of plus and minus.

Thus, the terms heaven and earth are necessary. The terms above and below, front and back, left and right are necessary. So, who is the center of heaven and earth? It is centered around me. Furthermore, the terms above and below, left and right, front and back all revolve around me. Ultimately, everything is centered around me. In this way, the pursuit of the highest standard of personhood and the pursuit of one world is not what God pursues; it is what I pursue. Thus, humanity becomes the center of the universe. Therefore, the unity of God and humanity occurs, and at the same time, the wishes of God and the wishes of humanity become one. God also has wishes. What is this wish? It is a point of unity. Ultimately, it is the same. Hence, it is said to be the person of heaven (天之人). This is the path that humanity must inevitably walk. Here, there are betrayers and victors.

So, who is a betrayer? Is it someone who has a bit of money? No matter how much money I have, that money remains in the Republic of Korea. Even if I betray, that money remains in the Republic of Korea. From this perspective, who is the owner of the money? It is not me. The Republic of Korea is the owner. I am merely a temporary manager, borrowing and using it. If I was born in the Republic of Korea, I live and pass through this land; I do not bring this land with me to live. Therefore, it does not start from oneself; it is always borrowed.

In borrowing, whether the borrower uses it for themselves or for the Republic of Korea is the issue. If I borrowed money for myself but take it away to use for the Republic of Korea, is that person a betrayer? What do you think? Here, differences arise depending on mindset and perception.

So, what does humanity desire? It desires the highest personhood and one world. In other words, it seeks an absolute person and an absolute world; both aspects are pursued by everyone.
Therefore, you live relying on people. It is not the workplace that you rely on. Men rely on women, and women rely on men; they rely on each other. Thus, each individual is a representative who relies on the world. The fact that the two rely on each other represents how people in the world rely on one another. Here, the degree to which you establish relationships with people scattered throughout the world determines your success. It is within this foundation that terms like betrayer and benefactor arise.

Do not become a betrayer of the heart.
From this perspective, there are two types of betrayers. Right? There are the external betrayers of the world and the internal betrayers of the heart; these are the two types of betrayers. However, external matters in the world are divided into countless branches. Looking at South Korea, there are executive departments, and beneath them, various organizations and businesses are divided into many branches. Even those who are responsible for these departments can experience betrayal in their work. However, this is because the person in charge is ignorant. Therefore, the issue is how to handle it. This raises the question of whether the person who betrayed is truly a betrayer. This is the nature of the betrayer in the external relative world.

However, there is no way to deal with the betrayer in the realm of the heart. A betrayer of the heart is one who betrays based not on material conditions but on emotional or vital conditions. Until now, what has Heaven been advocating? It has been advocating centered on emotional and vital conditions. When you have poured out your heart for someone, yet they do not recognize it, you can become a betrayer with just a word. This is not the case in the material world. In working with millions or even billions of won, you cannot label someone a betrayer over a matter of tens of thousands of won.

However, in the spiritual world, in the context of life's connections, it is urgent. A single word can completely sever the ties with someone who was once close and easily label them a betrayer. This is serious. Ultimately, the internal matters are of a serious degree that is broad, deep, and high.

Then, when we look at the two types of betrayers, in what aspect should we not become betrayers? We must not become betrayers in the realm of the heart. Even if you are branded as an external betrayer, if you unite in the realm of the heart, you can transcend the content of worldly betrayers pursuing the external world. If your heart is united, you cannot be labeled a betrayer just because you caused a business worth millions or tens of millions of won to fail. Even if you are in the same position, you cannot become a betrayer.

Here, the external matters are not serious. That is not the problem. The issue is the relationship among true people who are connected by internal feelings. If those who believe pursue absolute character centered on feelings and if they become estranged, they will part forever. Without possessing a higher spiritual content, a deeper emotional content, and a richer vital content, they cannot meet.

Even a devoted son who has built a filial piety monument for his parents will leave an eternal scar in the hearts of his parents if he speaks a single disrespectful word to them. "Ah! I did not know," he would exclaim, shocked as if the heavens and earth had turned upside down. This is how it is in the world of the heart.

The fundamental reason humans became enemies of God.
In your faith life, what is the problem? It is life and emotional matters. Therefore, what is the most precious thing to a person? In conclusion, it is not the external world. It is one's own life and heart. Here, the words filial piety, loyalty, and joy arise. The joy of receiving the resurrection of life, the joy of welcoming a day of life's ecstasy, the joy of discovering something higher and more precious in emotional terms—this happiness, this joy, is indeed better than any joy in the external world. This is the path that humans must take to establish their original posture.

The enemy of man is truly ambiguous. Right? Even among millionaires doing business together, they often compete and take each other's lives. Looking at the history of most countries, there is a history woven with battles of killing and being killed. From an external perspective, it seems to be a struggle over land, but internally, it is a struggle over love. You must understand that these two struggles have woven history together.

Where do feelings of sorrow and joy come from? They arise from these two forms of struggle. When someone fails, in what sense did they fail? Even if they say they have failed, they can still boldly say, "I can do greater things tomorrow with hope." If they take this as a stimulus and a turning point, they can become a hopeful victor tomorrow. Are they a failure? They have not failed. Rather, it becomes a new motivation and a new start. It is merely a stimulus for independence. In other words, it is just a process for a new beginning. It is not failure. Therefore, those who see it as failure are the ones who have failed, while those who do not see it that way are not failures. History has flowed this way.

Then, in such a society, where should we head? The issues of life and spirit are serious. Where did the enmity between God and man begin? Did it begin with eating the fruit of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil?

Even if a wealthy person in South Korea with tens of millions or billions of won loses all their wealth at once and becomes a beggar with nothing, they can overcome it. If they have internal content, they can overcome it. What they lost is not the issue; they can transcend it.

However, in the relationship between God and man, where did the resentment of the betrayer arise? It arose from a psychological relationship. It was not the fruit of the tree that could determine the fate of heaven and earth. So what is it?

From the subjective standpoint, what does God hope for? It is something newer, something more joyful, something more desirable, and something more lovable. God demands humans who can be like that. Such people must possess content in both life and spiritual matters. External material does not possess such content.

Humans have clashed with God over emotional issues. This was the first clash in history. As beings created by God, they were in a position where they could not even dream of such a thing, yet they betrayed Him. Did they do this hoping for a clash? They never even thought of it, yet such events occurred. Therefore, we must seek this out.

From this perspective, could it not be that the fall is a matter of emotional misalignment, as our Unification Church states? This is true both inductively and in observing social phenomena.

Is the spirit first, or is the material first?
Then, in this world, where are we heading between the inner world and the outer world? The external world and the internal world must gradually become one world. All issues of the external and internal worlds must be resolved in relation to humanity. This is a matter of heaven and earth. Therefore, heaven and earth must unite to form one external world, and thus, the internal unity of one personality must be achieved to finally embody the original world that God sought. Finding the internal personality that had not been wounded, which God desired before creating Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden, was God's wish.

From this perspective, what should we do? Here, the issue of social life as believers arises. It is important to have a mindset that values ultimate purpose rather than merely seeking success.

The future world depends on the youth. Those who have entered the Unification Church seem to know this well, but when the teacher asks, there is much they do not know. Some may ask, "Is it necessary to be so particular?" but it is not so.

Your inner world began before you were born. Likewise, your external world also began before you were born. Then, did this universe come into existence without any thought? No. Even for this piano to exist, there had to be content that made it possible. Although we do not know how it came into being, it certainly came into existence due to some harmonious force acting upon it. In other words, something acted upon it, resulting in its manifestation. Therefore, a material object is not the cause but the result.

When you were born, which came first, the emotional origin or the material origin? When I was born, both this world and my heart existed. So which came first? It cannot be that material came first.

The internal betrayal is greater than the external betrayal.
Centered on these issues, two major philosophical currents have formed: "the spirit is first" and "the material is first," with each side claiming to be right. 

Then can you say, "I will go without having a spirit"? No, you cannot. You think first and then act. That is how it is, isn't it? Even when eating, can you say, "I will eat"? You think, "I should eat," and then you eat. When you look at this, which comes first? The internal, that is, thinking comes first.

Then, which is greater for you, the desires of the body or the desires of the heart? The desires of the body have limits, just as you feel full after eating one more bowl of rice. However, the desires of the heart have no limits. So which is greater? Is there a limit to the desires of the heart? The material desires, or bodily desires, have a boundary. But what demands beyond that boundary is the desire of the heart. This is something you can clearly recognize in your life.

From this perspective, it is undeniable that the external material world does not cause the physiological functions of animals; rather, there exists a higher origin, that is, an intangible existence that can act upon it. The fundamental problems of life can be resolved in this way.

Then, when I was born, what do I like? Of course, I like to eat. When a baby is born, it likes to drink its mother's milk. However, it does not only like to drink its mother's milk. It likes to see its mother as well. Ultimately, it drinks milk to enjoy seeing its mother. Therefore, the mother, having given so much, does not mind giving milk because she expects that the child will follow her as much as she has poured out her life and heart into them. This is the nature of their relationship.

From the mother's perspective, she gives infinitely because she wants to see her child. She treats her child in an absolute relationship, believing that the more she pours out her life and heart, the more the child will follow her. When viewed from the perspective of the child, it seems to be a material relationship, but when viewed from the perspective of the mother, it is the opposite. So, which side is the subject? The mother is the subject. Since the mother is in a position to give material things, she is the subject. It is all like that. Therefore, humans must walk the path of life centered on the higher desires among the two types of desires.

The desires of the external world are not true desires. The desires of the internal world are the true desires. The desires of the external world seek comfort. The internal desires transcend this level. The desires of the external world are divisive to a certain extent. The desires of the internal world are holistic. They are all-encompassing. Isn't that right? People often say, "All of my love." This is a desire centered on God. Because God is the center of the whole.

Therefore, it can be said that a betrayer from the internal perspective is a greater betrayer than a betrayer from the external perspective. So where did humans commit sin? It was not from the external perspective. As Christianity understands, eating the fruit of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil was not the sin. Will that continue to persist? It originated from issues of life and spirit. You cannot deny this.

In both men and women, the greatest enemy is the one who threatens their life. Right? Then who is the enemy of South Korea? It is those who threaten the life and death issues of South Korea. What comes next? Next are those who seek to take away South Korea's desires. Those who try to obstruct the desire to save the world are enemies. And those who block what South Korea loves the most are enemies. So who is the enemy of South Korea? What is being propagated from the North? They say that the South exploits. But what does South Korea want to do? It wants to love its people. However, they do not want to love the people; they want to exploit them, which is why they are our enemies.

Similarly, when we look at ourselves as individuals, who is my enemy? The one who threatens my life is my enemy. Next is the one who takes away what I like. But is that gold? It is always about people. If a mother has jewelry she brought when she got married or inherited from ancestors, and if her knowledge is about to die and she must be hospitalized, and the only thing left is that jewelry, would there be someone who says, "I would rather my son die than let go of this jewelry"? At that moment, that jewelry is not the issue. This shows that human life and love issues have a greater impact.

What kind of being is Satan?
If humans are like this, what about God? Who does God resemble? If we humans are the sons and daughters of God, then God must ultimately resemble us humans, right? Then what kind of being is God's enemy? It is a being that threatens God's existence while simultaneously threatening the lives of the sons and daughters whom God loves.

What is Satan? It is a being that threatens the life of someone who should enter heaven, trying to drag them into hell, while simultaneously imprisoning free individuals and threatening their lives. This is Satan. Moreover, Satan is the being that threatens the beloved sons and daughters of God. This is what an enemy is. An enemy consists of these two aspects. Wouldn't you agree? 

Since God is absolute, His life cannot be threatened, but if there is someone who threatens the life of His sons and daughters, and threatens the love of those sons and daughters, that person becomes God's enemy. Right? The enemy of the sons and daughters is the enemy of the parents, and the enemy of the parents is the enemy of the sons and daughters. There are cases where a mother or father, before dying, says to their children, "If I die, avenge me." If there is an enemy who killed their son, the father will take revenge. All of this revolves around threatening life and love. When you look at all of this, you come to feel that this is how it has become.

Then, who is God's betrayer? It is Satan. Therefore, we must understand this Satan. Who is the next betrayer? It is humanity. You might not feel good about this, right? Why did humanity become the enemy of God? It is as I mentioned earlier.
This is because humans could not establish a relationship with God regarding emotional issues and instead formed a relationship with Satan, being born as children of Satan. They could not become sons and daughters of God but became children of Satan.

Let me explain with an example. Do you know what a "min daughter-in-law" is? In a family that is not well-off, there is a son who cannot afford to marry freely, so he brings a poor girl from a neighboring house and raises her within his own fence, intending to pair her with his son when the time comes. This daughter-in-law is called a min daughter-in-law. However, if she is raised well as a min daughter-in-law and, when the time comes to pair them, she abandons the man and elopes with another young man from the village, would that create enmity? Yes, it would.

In the same way, God has become like this. The partner who was to become one with God's son has disappeared. There was only one woman who could be centered on God and become the ancestor of humanity. Here, Eve is in the position of a min daughter-in-law, and the archangel Lucifer has taken away Eve, the min daughter-in-law. Adam is the body of God. As stated in 1 Corinthians 3:16, "Do you not know that you are God's temple and that God's Spirit dwells in you?" Our bodies are the house of God. When Adam matures and is able to comprehend the world, that is, when God's house is fully built, God will enter that house. Then God and Adam will become one, within the house created by God.

The place where the Creator and the created can become one
God created the earth, the relative world, and humans. So what is our desire? To become the highest person, right? And to establish the highest world, right? And whose desire is that? It is God's desire. In other words, the standard of the highest personality we aspire to is God's desire, and the world we hope for is God's desire, who created heaven and earth. Because we are to be born as the original person who should receive such things, we also have the purpose of completing the personality that God desired, that is, the personality of Adam and Eve, so we pursue the highest personality. Furthermore, since the relative world was created centered on that personality, we must govern the world of all things. That is God's desire.

Now, when God enters Adam, do God's desire and Adam's desire become two or one? "They become one." That is how it works. It becomes both Adam's desire and God's desire. God wishes to govern this created world by becoming one with the highest personal being, that is, to embrace all things in His bosom. Therefore, we humans also become one with the highest person and one with the highest world. When we enter into a subjective position where we can become one like this, the relative world is established.

This is where the term "heaven and earth united" comes from. The place where the Creator and the created can become one is nowhere else. To become one like this, all internal and external qualities must match, right? They must match to become one. If one side is slightly thicker, can they be together forever? Even if they come together, one will fall away because it is heavier. It is destined to fall apart, not to rise together. In movement, if both are the same, they will take a parallel course.

Therefore, if God created humans with the intention of becoming one, and since God is absolute, the person born using the body of the absolute must establish a relative standard that can support the absolute God. This is possible through the human heart. The human heart can carry God. The human heart has that capability. It can carry God as much as it wants.

Is your heart narrow or wide? You may not know the shape of your heart very well, but the heart is infinitely large. So how good is that heart? It is a heart that wants to give hundreds of billions of won to each of the 3 billion people in the world and still wants to give more. Isn't that right? The heart is that wonderful. Therefore, humans can bloom as flowers of infinite love and infinite hope. Why is that? Because they resemble the infinite nature of God. When we look at the heart and body, the heart is large, but the body is small. Thus, the heart and body are always in a relative relationship. This is how they stimulate each other. That is why I feel joy or sadness. Therefore, it is inevitable that a relative relationship must be established.

The path a pure religious person must take
What happened to Eve, who is a min daughter-in-law? She formed a relationship with a servant. This is the fall. She formed a relationship with a servant. We, the descendants of fallen humans, have received the blood of Satan. It is astonishing.

Therefore, who is the traitor before God today? It is Satan and his descendants. Then, from God's perspective, how should He repay the enemy? Shouldn't He cut off the enemy's neck? That is how it should be, right? Then, whose neck should He cut off first? "Satan's." He should cut off Satan's neck and then cut off the neck of humans, right? If He cannot cut off the necks of the enemy, Satan and humans, then God would be defeated, so He must cut them off, right?

However, from God's perspective, should He repay the enemy or not? This is concerning. The stage has been set like this. From here, the path a pure religious person must take emerges. So what is the path a pure religious person must take? Should they repay the enemy or forgive the enemy? This is the issue. God is in a position where He is confronted with such a dilemma.

God created the universe with all His heart, dreaming of a hopeful great work, but when all those great works and conditions of life and ideals were shattered and destroyed at once, the heavens and earth became dark. The archangel Lucifer appeared as the enemy here. Should God capture and punish Lucifer, or not? Lucifer took God's beloved children, who are bone of His bone and flesh of His flesh, as his own children. Should He cut off the neck of such an enemy or leave it be? This is the first time in history that God has agonized over such a question.

In today's human world, the enemies who threaten their lives and love are not the issue. The first being who experienced such sorrow and suffering in history, who struggled to overcome the misery of that history, is God. God is at a crossroads of whether to take up the sword or choose the law of forgiveness. Isn't that right? If He takes up the sword and kills, it will leave a lasting aftermath for thousands and millions of years. In doing so, it would ultimately mean that He is killing His own sons and daughters. Although they have received the blood of the enemy, they are different from the children of the world. The father raised that daughter with care from childhood, intending to make her his daughter-in-law, but she formed a relationship with a thug out of nowhere. Yet that daughter is acting as if she is thrilled, doing all sorts of things. God finds this even more frustrating.

Adam and Eve are the first sons and daughters, and they are God's body. They were created to establish the substantial world as future gods. God does not create that world alone.

Would you be happy if you were alone? Does a person's heart feel joy when alone? Does a man feel joy when alone? There must be a counterpart. Why did God create heaven and earth? He created them to find a counterpart. No existing church or religion can answer this. Ultimately, God created the universe to live a life of joy. Therefore, Adam is the body of God. Then who is Eve? She is Adam's wife, so she is the object of God. Thus, Adam and Eve become the origin of the entire creation and the origin of all life. Therefore, we must repay the enemy, Satan, who threatened this.

Therefore, we were born as children of the enemy.
