What does this have to do with you? How much has God worked hard to relate that? How much has He struggled to cross the path of the enemy and lay the foundation to command through one person? Even though there is a grievance of countless years centered on the will of reconciliation, you think of it as ordinary.

Among those with strong patriotism, many have connections with the Unification Church. The teacher can know what kind of spirit world they are related to. They are following what I have done until now.

Now, since we must restore the world, we must embrace all those who are in the spirit world. To do that, we cannot use means. When he is serious, I must be more serious than he is. This is the fight we have been engaged in until now. When you see someone who claims to be in the spirit world, you just bow your head, but that should not be the case. Your heart should not be like that. Being in the spirit world is simple.

From this perspective, we must move forward centered on the global will. How much has God prepared for us, who go to the front lines of restoration on behalf of such people? You must understand how much He has struggled to love the children of enemies. If you know this value and become a son who cares about God's noble sacrifice, you cannot complain, no matter how difficult it is.

Jesus knew how much God had worked hard for four thousand years to support the betraying nation of Israel, and because he knew that the desire for himself was great, he could not complain from the position of a son. Ultimately, he was in a position to ask the Father to forgive them. That is why Jesus was a filial son. There was no man like Jesus. There was not a single woman like that. Therefore, Jesus must come again to find such a woman. That is how the conclusion is reached.

Thus, in the midst of the love connection between God and humanity, new sons and daughters of reality will appear. From there, the world of God centered on the original love of creation will be realized. That is why we are told to love our enemies. Have you loved your enemies? Can you like them or not?

To make a betrayer true
That is why Jesus sought out three disciples and established twelve disciples, and he tried to govern the children of enemies with the power of love by establishing the nation of Israel. Only then will the name of betrayer disappear from this earth. A place without betrayers is heaven. Therefore, the question is whether you will always unravel the path of evil in front of a good heart or expel evil. We must save the evil people.

That is why Jesus said, "I have come to heal the sick, not the healthy. I have not come to save the righteous, but to save sinners." How can we love the children of enemies without having a heart that sympathizes with the position of sinners? Therefore, we must always think from the position of the other party.

Jesus also had to think from that position. So how shocking it must have been! "Isn't the Son of Man the Son of God? Shouldn't I originally be in the position of a child of God? Then why has it come to this? Wasn't I originally a child of God? Then why has it come to this?" Jesus had to re-examine that. You must know how much he lamented over the world he lost. You do not even know that. Since you do not know that, I have the responsibility to teach you. If I have taught everything and you betray, you are a betrayer, but if you betray from a position of not knowing because I did not teach you, that is not betrayal. Therefore, not being able to teach is a sin.

The fact that the Republic of Korea betrays also comes from not knowing the principle. Therefore, we must say they are betraying after teaching them. However, we must not teach them incorrectly. If you teach them clearly and they still betray, they will face judgment. Until you teach them, you must love them. You must love them more than yourself. God has carried out such providential work even to this extent.

Because Jesus died through Israel, he must return to the miserable Israel. Since God stood on the side of Israel and brought them out, and Israel has gone astray, Jesus must come back to Israel again. In other words, there remains a foundation to return centered on Christianity, the second Israel. If he had abandoned everything on this earth, he would not be able to come back.

Therefore, because you know this content, which is the hope of humanity, we will never perish. If God withdraws the will of providence, we will perish, but because that does not happen, we will never perish. Therefore, we must stand in the position of the other party and worry one hundred percent. There is a reason for everything the other party does.

When I was in prison, I was with prisoners who had been sentenced to death. When I talked to them, they all had their own miserable circumstances.
This means that it can be so. When we look at humanity itself, it can be so. However, the direction was different. If we clarify that position where the direction changed, we can turn back.

You must understand this content and become individuals who can genuinely understand the position of the other party from the standpoint of true parents, standing in the position of true children with the heart of love. By doing so, you will know that you can escape the position of the betrayer and should move forward with sincerity in that regard.

Loving your enemy is the greatest struggle for you. Even in evangelism, you must do it with that heart. Those who go beyond that will never fail. If such a person is made to starve, that neighborhood will perish. On the other hand, wherever such a person goes, an enemy will surely appear. It is a test to see if that person is truly such a person or not. If they pass that test, it will be revealed that they are a good person.

When you enter the Unification Church, there are personal enemies, family enemies, tribal enemies, and national enemies. And nowadays, the world is an enemy. The American government is currently a problem for the teacher. It is a problem globally. Countries like Japan and all around the world are making me a problem. The teacher has become the man of the issue. Externally, it may be a problem for them, but internally, it does not affect me. No matter how much they make it an enemy, the world of results that appears externally is flowing away. However, no matter what they say, in the emotional world, they will perish, not me.

Move from the world of Satan to the world of heaven. 

Because this is certain, the teacher prayed in front of the White House with that meaning. Do you understand what I mean? I cannot speak of the content of that prayer, but it was not a prayer for America to perish.

If you want to walk this path, the question is how you should organize yourselves. You must gather your hearts once again and fight on.

When you move, you organize your belongings and pack them up, right? Similarly, you must organize everything and move. Those who live in the world of death will perish. Therefore, you must move. Where should you move? You must go from the world of Satan to the world of heaven. And in the kingdom of God, you must throw away all trivial things and take only the good.

When you get married, can you bring what your husband dislikes? You must bring what your husband likes. Similarly, when you move, you must take only the good. Only then will the time come when you can leave behind the history of betrayers and live very happily in the kingdom of heaven.

<Prayer> Father, we know that you do not wish for me to be far from you. When we are here, you want to be here with us, and when we go there, you want to go there too. We know that your heart is to always be together, to live together, and to die together. This is like the heart of a human wanting to be with, live with, and die with their own children. Since our such heart began from you, we must also be like that.

Father! Have we ever been so desperate to long for you, putting forth our utmost sincerity, stretching out our arms and crying out to you as our Father? If not, we are shameful children.

Have I ever run with busy feet for your will? If I have not, we are shameful children. How many times have we struggled with your will in our hearts, searching for the path of hope, only to collapse? If we have not done that, we must discover ourselves as sinners before you.

When have we loved you so madly that we forsook everything in the world, or cursed everything and cast it away, and when have we longed for your love so much that we could not sleep at night and struggled?

Now we realize how much you have struggled to find us before we did that.

It turns out that much time has passed. It turns out we have become shameless beings. It turns out that we are in a position where we must again be reminded of the story of restoration by you, so please forgive us.

We learned about your situation regarding the nation through fighting with the nation, and we realized it through fighting with the world. Yet, we have come to know that the most pitiful person is you, and the loneliest person is also you, and that you are the one who has walked the path of death a thousand or ten thousand times. Before such a Father, we have come to understand that even if we die a million times, are trampled a million times, chased a million times, and find ourselves in a million unjust positions, we must still embrace you.

Until now, we did not know that such a high and precious being is closer to us than our own parents and siblings. When we realize that you are at the center of life more than anyone else, please allow us to discover the joy of dedicating everything for one day of your glory.

Let us know that this is a meaningful life and that this is a valuable life.

No matter how much the world mocks and insults us, that is just a passing moment. As we look forward to the day when those mocking us will bow their heads in repentance, we must become the children of unity who strive to maintain the attitude of being your sons.

What do your sons and daughters gathered here this morning seek? What do they desire? It is to stand on your side, to hold onto your hem and go through the rough path, and even if we must die, to die in your embrace. Is that not our wish? We must walk that path.

On the way for the nation, enemies still stand in our way. We must repent for our sins of not loving the nation. There are walls blocking the way to the world. Help us to realize that we must walk that path, having discovered that we have not sacrificed and struggled for the world.

We have come to know that the path of loving our enemies and tracing your heart is a lonely path. That path is one where tears do not cease, where the arrows of the enemy do not stop, and where mockery, criticism, and scorn do not cease. This is the history you have had to navigate, so please allow us to understand that we must also endure it.

We sincerely hope and desire to become sons and daughters who strive to be able to find your heart while experiencing beauty in suffering, injustice, sadness, and anger.

Father, the year 1969 is coming to an end. The year 1970 is the third year of the second seven-year course. Your children gathered here must fulfill their responsibilities.

We know that we have a responsibility to settle the debts owed to you and the debts owed to our ancestors in our lifetime and to bear fruit and expand this horizontally before our tribe and nation. We earnestly ask that you allow us to be your children who strive solemnly to fulfill that mission.

Please allow us to be children who once again pledge to be faithful stewards in front of the remaining will, and we pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

3) The Importance of Family Life

<Summary of the Words> Generally, when one is alone, they do not fail. They fail when they are in relation to others. Therefore, a solitary life is absolutely necessary. Minimize external contact and expand the internal world.

We are not individual-centered but family-centered. However, that does not mean that we settle everything solely based on the family; everything must be interconnected. Therefore, the efforts made in the past when one lived alone are not sufficient. We must attach a resolution and determination to work several times harder than we did in the past.

Living a life that challenges evil can easily lead to exhaustion and retreat. When one has a family, they must exert several times more effort than when they were alone.

The family is the place where the center is held. We cannot escape reality. We must establish relationships in all directions—front and back, left and right, up and down—within the family.

We cannot rely on past forms of faith. We cannot have a one-sided faith attitude from the past.

Blessing is the decisive point of life and death.

An individual's faith can be maintained as long as they meet a good leader. However, in a family, everyone must become a leader for one another.

The question is for whom and for what do we live in the family?

On November 26, 1969 (Wednesday), at the former headquarters church.
* These words were spoken after the evening service and are compiled from notes taken by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Historical Compilation Committee. The title was added by the editor.

When one is alone, prayer can accomplish everything. However, in a family, if there are opposing individuals, one must bear that cross and push through to the original standard.

Being alone is like a passenger car, while a family is like a locomotive. It is simple to restore what an individual has erred in. However, if there is a family error, it leads to disaster.

You know you must walk this path and do this work. But when will you do it? 

Do you have confidence in life? Do you have confidence in overcoming evil? Do you have confidence in becoming a child of God? Can someone who lacks confidence in their own life defeat Satan, the main force of evil that has been melting God for six thousand years?

In the 1960s, the teacher lived to establish the foundation of the church. Now, what will you do in the 1970s, and what will you do in the 1980s? What will you accomplish in these 20 years? You must find that position recognized by God.

The assurance of my life lies in heaven. Those who live for public purposes are recorded in heaven's book of life. Ultimately, Satan will lose before God. Therefore, even if we cannot strike evil immediately, we can carry the victory.

In a family, there is much spiritual consumption. Therefore, those who have a deep foundation of faith from a young age are happy. One must enter a deep level of faith even for just five seconds to live. If one continues to consume without replenishing, they will perish.

When one is alone, it is simple, but after having a family, it is not so. One must make efforts that are not known to others. How do you obtain that resource? There is no other way but prayer. Even if it is just during the dawn worship time, let us stand in a straight line with heaven. That time is truly serious. If you are even one second late during that time, repent. During that time, prepare even a single candy as an offering and distribute it to the children, just as during communion...

The family is important. If one fails, they cannot be supplemented. When a young man and woman meet and fall in love, they tend to forget everything, including ideals. We must recognize that the family is the starting point of everything. If everyone only claims their own opinions and fights, the nation will perish, and heaven and earth will perish. The family is like a breathing hole for us.

Only after establishing the dignity of heaven can we establish our own and the other's dignity. No matter how much you love your husband or wife, if it goes against principle, you must correct each other.

You must pray. You must make offerings. You must make offerings of the heart and of life. To do this, pray. Get up early and pray. When you pray, you must be able to hear the sound of your heartbeat. Imagine that the harmony of heaven and earth unfolds from the arteries and veins, and think of the source of your heart. Then your health will improve.

Praise heaven centered on the nature of creation. Then you will not feel lonely wherever you go. Even if you are alone, you will never feel lonely.

Shouldn't you become a furnace to be warm?

When you long for the invisible and feel its reality, that is eternal.

Worry about the will, not about business. No matter how exhausted you are, if you retreat without reaching the destination you have worked hard for, you are a fraud. Even if you must die, you must die heading toward that place. When you work, you must work for that purpose. You cannot retreat without having seen heaven.

Why can’t you work hard and sweat? Let us work hard so that future generations can commemorate and be proud of us.

We have come to find the family to establish the kingdom of heaven. If you turn back saying you cannot go, you will perish. It is fine for individuals to perish, but the path of the will must not be blocked. You are blocking that path.

You are in the position of the Messiah, who must fight and achieve.

It is not unfortunate that living conditions are difficult. The question of how closely you can approach heaven in secret is the crossroads of happiness and unhappiness.

It is fine for individuals to perish, but families must not perish.

For a husband, the wife is the most needed person in the world, and for a wife, the husband is the most needed person. They must encourage each other and become a staff and co-worker.

You must pray while doing laundry and while walking. The storehouse must keep piling up; it must not be empty.

If parents do their utmost to avoid straying from the path to heaven, their children will never be unfilial.

How can we live exemplary lives for three generations? That is the question.

What will you do if Satan takes your children? You must create many allies who can protect them. To do this, you must evangelize.

You must repeatedly live a life of prayer, reflection, and resolution. If you do not evangelize your friends and go to the other world, you will be accused there. Therefore, you must evangelize diligently. Even when the teacher is insulted, you must pray. All of this is because you are at fault...

You must give thanks even after being hit by your husband. 

As a husband, can you not hit your wife even once? Thank you.

Without a life of constant prayer, you cannot walk the path of the will. In your life, do not think about money first; think about the will first.

The wife of a leader must never complain when her husband leaves the house. When a wife complains, it clouds the heart of her husband, and that wave clouds the world. Complaints should be made in the evening. Then all problems will be resolved overnight. A man goes out in the morning to fight. For such a husband, the wife should wake up early and provide good service.

Even if you must apply perfume and fix your makeup, women should always be beautiful. Women should not be in debt in emotional life. They should also always pay attention to their husband's body and clothing. When the husband comes home looking tired, prepare a basin of water for him to wash his face, get ready for him to brush his teeth, wash his feet, and comb his hair. A woman's smile is the flower of the home. To create a harmonious family, a woman must become the best actress in both joy and sorrow, melting completely when her husband is happy and melting completely when he is sad.

How much do you love your children?

You should change your clothes at least once every three days. You should wash your hair that often too. And always wear a smile. A smile is the flower of the heart. Always bloom flowers and spread fragrance.

You should know how to test your partner with your hairstyle or makeup. If you cannot please your partner with your face or appearance, you should compensate with hobbies. Try to mobilize music and all forms of art. It is also good to explain women's physiology after reading magazines or literature. Let your husband live like a child wrapped in your skirt.

Once a couple meets, they should hold each other’s arms and go together, whether in life or death. Since we are going, let’s go in style.
Pray. Prayer is the supply depot of the heart. Even if you don't have time, you can pray through the work you do. *

The Resolve of a Believer
<Prayer> Father, this morning, we wish to feel your desire to be with your children gathered here and to walk together with them. Please allow us to experience this at this time.
From the time of sorrow that you endured because of the ancestors of humanity until today, we must once again recall the effort you have made to find the path of restoration.
We must think once more about how much the sons and daughters you longed for have broken your heart, how much they have struck your body, and how much they have driven you to a pitiful place.
Father, it is increasingly painful to think that the reason you have been placed in such an unjust and furious position is not because of you, but because of the people on this earth who are connected to your children. Even in such circumstances, we reflect on your heart that could not abandon your sons and daughters, and your situation that could not forget them. Please surely reunite those sons and daughters to fulfill your will and bring about reconciliation.
Those sons and daughters must be presented as a condition of praise before all creation, and they must raise their hands to praise your high and preciousness, responding to the gifts of glory. We know that it is your wish and will for all people to become such sons and daughters.

We also understand that knowing this means we must fulfill the responsibilities for it.

We must recognize that whether we look to heaven or earth, or anything else, we exist in a position of value that we can be grateful for and boast about.
Father, we hope that your love, which we cannot sever, will always dwell in our hearts. We know that this loving heart earnestly wishes to fully govern our living sphere. We must understand your heart and situation, which desires us to participate in the place where your will remains alongside the history of the eternal world and to be with us in our path of life to guide us. Please allow us to become heavenly warriors who can dedicate our lives before you. Is there a new command and promise of yours that must be established on this earth? This morning, may you be present wherever we gather, and may you grant a thousandfold blessings to your children who are concerned and praying for this place.

Today is November 30, 1969, the last Sabbath of this month. Father, please bless this day that we cannot meet again, and be with us as we move toward the end of understanding. <Words> We know that among the humans living on this earth, there are not many who have the confidence that they can win forever by themselves. Even when we look at a day's life, we know well that life is one in which we live believing and hoping for something without even knowing it.
What we believe and hope for
When we head to our workplaces or responsible departments in the morning, we inevitably approach our daily lives with a heart that prays and hopes. If a day is like that, a month will be so, a year will be so, and our life journey will also be so.
93 
From this perspective, just as individuals are like this, so too are nations and the world. Since individuals are connected to form a nation and a world, we can see that if our personal lives carry a heart of desire and hope, then a nation will be the same, and a world will be the same. If there is an absolute being who created this universe, then that absolute being will also be the same. Not only we humans but also God, who resides in the heavenly world, has a heart that hopes and desires something.
When we look at the present moment, what is it that humans or God hope for and long for? What do they pursue? We cannot deny the fact that they wish for something better than reality. They hope that the time that comes after this moment will be better than the time up to now, and that the future position will be better than the current position. It is here that the issue of faith arises.
What we believe and hope for is not something realistic. It is a future issue. The very essence of desire is not realistic. It is a matter that will inevitably confront us after going through the process of time. Therefore, all the hearts that we wish for or believe in can be better than our current position and seek to add something to our present position.
Thus, if I have the strength of ten in the present and wish for something of greater value, something greater than ten, then there must be a strength greater than ten in the place I am pursuing. If I wish for ninety from the position of ten, then the question is how to achieve ninety. It is impossible to fulfill the desired wish without adding a strength of ninety to my position of ten. This is an undeniable fact.
Today, we humans are limited in many ways. Therefore, we cannot freely navigate issues of life and death or happiness and unhappiness. Is there anyone who does not wish to be happy? Is there anyone who wants to end in misery? However, the path of fate cannot be resolved by oneself. The overall issues of happiness, unhappiness, or life and death are indeed unfolding around humans, but humans themselves cannot be the solution to all these problems.
Considering this fact, when we think about how to overcome the threshold of death or unhappiness, we find that unhappiness must be in a position lower than the current point where one stands, or if one possesses a strength of ten, they must inevitably find themselves in a position lower than that strength of ten, which ultimately becomes a disadvantage to oneself. To avoid this, the question becomes where to receive factors that can add to the strength of ten. This is an absolute requirement that must be demanded in our lives.
The Standard a Believer Should Look To
To believe and move forward with one's desired wish, one must have a greater driving force than that wish. Without it, one cannot achieve that wish. In this light, pushing through unhappy environments or the threshold of death to attain a happy environment or eternal life is not such a simple matter. When humans, who are confined within limited boundaries, seek something beyond that, they cannot be the motive for everything because they are not the motive itself, and thus they cannot help but seek the power of a motive that can resolve all things.
For this reason, before we wish to fulfill our desires, we must seek something that can realize those desires, which is pursued not by relative standards but by higher standards. This is where the issue of faith arises in our inner world and daily lives.
So, when we say that we have made a new resolution and have a new resolve centered on the standard of faith to achieve our purpose, our position is no longer the previous one. We are not in a position that relates to the environment we have lived in until now and are currently living in. We will stand in a position centered on some absolute standard that transcends the current position and relative position. When you stand in such a position, you can see a new beginning from there. Therefore, the standard a believer should look to is the absolute God. It is not relative us. The resolve of a believer begins from God's side. Without such an absolute standard, we cannot discern the conditions of happiness and unhappiness and move toward the ideals we desire.
Therefore, whether a ruler responsible for a nation or a politician responsible for the world, when they look at the reality of the nation or world they manage and oversee, they come to realize that the more complex the content of that world is, the more they feel their own limitations and recognize that they cannot do anything with their own strength. The more significant the task they take on, the fewer people there are who believe they can accomplish it solely with their surroundings and abilities. Thus, they inevitably pursue some relative factors that can empower them, some absolute standard of strength. They hope that that strength will manifest itself beyond their current strength. The result is that they wish for something beyond their current position. This position cannot be avoided. What is found beyond one's environment becomes the motive, and through that, one must bear fruit to feel a new desire and a new victorious pleasure.
For this reason, the position that pursues motives beyond realistic standards and results beyond realistic standards, that is, the position that hopes for and pursues something better than reality, is precisely the position of a believer. In other words, it is the way of life of a believer. When we look at it this way, what is the way of life of a believer? It is to bring about relative results from a position of strength, motive, and place that is greater than oneself. This is the issue.
Today, we must not remain in a limited environment. We must transcend that limited realm. To transcend, one cannot rely solely on one's own strength. Therefore, the more one confronts such a position, the more sincerity is required. When we look at the resolve of a believer, sincerity is essential in making that resolve. The very decision that says, "I will now do it," that is, the determination centered on the goal as a believer, must also be made with sincerity. That sincerity must not be based solely on the content of habitual living environments up to now but must be based on a higher standard.
The Way of Life of a Believer
So, what must we do? We must focus all our senses on that. And we cannot live a habitual life. We must live beyond that. In other words, we must concentrate all our sensory organs, such as sight, hearing, and touch, on one center. Unless we prepare a foundation that can unify and concentrate there, we cannot transcend our current position.
Thus, the Bible also says, "Love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, with all your strength, and with all your mind" (Luke 12:30). The command to do so contains a universal content. The question arises as to which area one is doing so. In a family, when a wife gives her heart to her husband, it can be said that she has done so from her position. However, can that wife's position represent the whole? No, it cannot.
A part of the whole cannot represent the whole. It is not absolute. To stand in an absolute position as a wife, one must rise to a relative position that aligns with God's presence and the standards that God desires, which are God's absolute standards. From such a standpoint, we are called to love the Lord your God with all your heart, all your soul, and all your strength. This is the first commandment that Jesus spoke of. This commandment is an absolute factor that can fulfill our desires, that is, what we wish for. Therefore, the place where believers go is not a place that can be determined by circumstances that can be criticized within your living environment today. That place is a realm that is connected in a tangible, transcendent state.

Thus, making a new resolution as a believer and living under that resolution is not a simple matter. That place is the highest place, the peak. It is like a watershed. In moving toward that highest place, one should not lean to the left or right but should compare the front and back, and one must rise rather than descend.

The position that a believer should take is extremely simple if it is simple, and it is the most complex if it is complex. It can be said to be simple because it goes straight toward a single goal. However, if one falls due to a mistake, various complications arise. Therefore, if it is complex, it can be said to be incomprehensibly complex.

The path that we believers are on is a path toward the peak. When heading directly toward that peak, that is, toward that goal, it is simple. When one discards everything except what is necessary to head toward the goal and goes solely for that goal, it is simple. However, if what one wishes for is not absolute but relative, then insurmountable problems arise. There, infinite complexity intervenes.

Therefore, believers must always look toward that realm. When stepping out in the morning, one must think about where one's heart and daily goals will be directed. Thus, when returning in the evening or going to bed after a day, one should be able to say, "Today was good. I accomplished everything today. I could stand before my purpose. Today can represent this month and can be a source of pride for this year."

One must stand in a position where one can do that. Without fierce struggle, one cannot stand in such a position. 

You are breathing now, but you often do not feel it. It is an undeniable fact that your heart is beating, yet you do not feel it in your daily life. Do you feel your eyes blinking regularly? Of course, you feel it when you blink, but you do not think about it in your daily life. All these things are undeniable facts in themselves, yet we do not feel them.

But if God is said to be among us, can we acknowledge that? Even if undeniable truths surround us, we must strive to recognize them. Can you feel that God is deep within your heart? You can feel some things that are visible and tangible if you concentrate, but can you recognize that God is deep in His heart, which is invisible? Without focusing your mind, it is hard to recognize. Does that mean God does not exist? No. He certainly exists.

God does not want to guide us down the path of unhappiness but rather wants to lead us down the path of maximum happiness. Is there any part of your body that desires to go to a painful place? No. Every part of your body wishes to be in a comfortable position and acts to align with that. Therefore, when you enter an uncomfortable place, you know immediately. You know right away when you find yourself in a place with polluted air.

In the same way, when there are unpleasant things in the path toward seeking God, you know immediately. That is called conscience. Therefore, there cannot be a religion that says it is okay to live a life of faith while being tormented by conscience. There can be religious doctrines that teach you to be stimulated and build relationships based on joy, comfort, and liberation of the heart, but there cannot be a religion that teaches you to stand in the opposite position.

To stand in a place where your heart can be at peace and joyful, you must transcend the ordinary and realistic life environment. You must be different from ordinary people. It is not about harmonizing with the various conditions of contemporary society. It is about transcending them. You must become the subject in that transcendence. Thus, you must lead people out. You must become a new subject. To become a new subject, you must establish a standard that your heart can lead.

Therefore, the starting point of a believer is not the external world but one's own conscience. Thus, faith is needed to discuss issues beyond one's conscience, not to discuss issues below it.

What does it mean to say that there is a higher position? For individuals, there is a limit they can reach as individuals. For men, there is a limit they can reach as one of the 1.5 billion men among 3 billion people. For women, there is also a limit they can reach as women. Additionally, when men and women come together to form a family, there is a limit they can reach as that family.

There will be such peaks. Each individual has a peak they must overcome. You also have peaks you must overcome, but those peaks are not flat. They are the highest points. In moving toward that, you should not try to go straight over the peak but rather follow the mountain range.

What is most needed for a believer? You are like a small mountain peak, and that mountain peak is connected through the mountain range that serves as its motivation. If you are the main peak that can lead all the mountain ranges, that is one thing, but if you are not in an absolute position, you must always be in a relative position, seeking something absolute. Since you are undoubtedly a small mountain peak, you must seek the main peak. 

As you ascend, your perspective changes. Until now, you could only see the village in the valley. You had no idea about the higher peaks beyond your current peak. Even if you want to know about that peak, you must receive teachings from that peak. To receive that teaching, you must absolutely comply. You must absolutely believe. Until you believe absolutely, you cannot understand even if you are taught.

When you go to school and study, if you are in university, when a professor stands at the podium and lectures, "This is how it is," students accept that content 100% because they believe in that professor, even if they have not experimented with it. They accept it from a position where all obstacles are removed, with the resolution to make all the content taught by the professor their own.

If someone says they cannot accept the professor's lecture, that is, if they cannot believe in that professor, they must become a professor themselves, spending decades on the podium to understand.

Therefore, a person on a lower peak must absolutely believe in the circumstances of a higher peak. Criticizing from here will not allow you to move beyond your current position. You cannot develop. To go beyond that, you must engage in infinite struggle. In other words, if the environment is prepared, and the path is all paved, you should be able to walk that paved path, but if you refuse to take that path and insist on finding your own way, you will have to struggle infinitely, and it will be nearly impossible.

So, when we look at our life path, how great is the purpose we must seek, the ultimate standard we desire? It is not the national standard of the Republic of Korea, nor is it the global standard of the world we currently live in. It is a standard that transcends history. That standard is what we refer to in the Unification Church as the heavenly principle. It is the pursuit of the value of humanity that encompasses the entire heaven and earth. If you do not believe in that high and precious value and insist on experimenting and knowing everything for yourself, you will not be able to go. You must believe. You must believe more than the other party asserts.

Then, if the person making that assertion collapses, you become the owner. The teacher has fought this battle until now.

That is why you are told to love the Lord your God with all your heart, all your soul, and all your strength. Here, where is the limit of "all"? It is to transcend history. It is to unite around a standard close to absolute authority, that is, to connect with the ultimate point and to give your all. That place is the position that God desires, the relative position toward God. In the Unification Church, such a position, such a point, is called God's heart.

The main peak of faith
A believer must move forward. In other words, one must follow the mountain range toward the main peak. There will be various paths toward that main peak. If there is a large mountain, there will be mountain ranges extending in all directions centered around the main peak. There may be mountain ranges that become cliffs in the middle, making it impossible to go further. There are mountain ranges of various shapes and colors.

So, where should we go today? 

If the path you need to take is blocked, no matter how hard you try to force your way through, you cannot pass that path. So what should you do? You must cross the current valley and climb another peak. To climb another peak, you must completely deny and clear away all the concepts, habitual lifestyles, and traditional contents you have held until now. Then, you must seek a path that can lead you directly toward the main peak.

A wise person, a thoughtful person, will find the closest path to the main peak. To find that path, what should you do? You should not insist on going alone. You must ask. If someone is climbing the mountain, you should ask them. If someone is ahead of you, you should ask, "How is the path you are taking?"

There are mountain ranges extending east, west, south, and north toward the main peak. However, there is only one closest path. In going toward the main peak centered around that path, even if you go down, it is not really going down. It is going up because you are heading toward the main peak. There will be trials and pains, and there will be crossroads of death. However, they are not there to bring you down but to refine you through confrontation. Therefore, on the day you overcome that, you will be able to find the main peak.

There are many such hurdles in going toward the main peak. Even if there are many hurdles, those who follow the mountain range extending from the main peak can go smoothly. However, if you should go east but are going west, you must turn back. You must turn 180 degrees in the opposite direction. If you cannot do that, it will not work. If a person in the west looks at the direction a person in the east is going and thinks, "That person is going that way, so I should go that way too," they will eventually go down. Thus, they will end up going in the opposite direction.
What is the biggest problem here? It is knowing the main peak. In other words,

one must know the destination to go to, the central purpose of faith. One must know God for certain. One must be sure whether God exists or not. A person who claims to walk the path of faith without knowing this is a foolish person. To practice faith, one must clearly know the destination and the center.  
Dear friends, even climbing Baegundae can lead to accidents, so what kind of path is the path of faith? The path of faith is a complicated one. It is the scariest path. If you make a mistake while walking, it is a path from which you cannot retreat and go back. That is the end. Once you start, you must go all the way. It is not a path you can take intermittently. If you fall once, you will suffer a great blow. A person who loses their strength in their faith life finds it difficult to recover. On a normal path, if a cliff blocks the way, you can take another route, but the path of faith is a great cliff if you fall, and there is no way to recover.  
Think of the ancient cultural nations. What happened when a nation that built a new culture centered on religion fell? That nation had no way to recover until it found the power of a new religion. When they set the culture that could dominate the world as the limit of their purpose and advanced, they might develop until they achieve that purpose, but once they stand at the place where they say, "Now it's enough," they fall. I have not directly explained what kind of person the teacher of the Unification Church is. You have provided evidence of what kind of person you are. A tail cannot pull the head. You might say it could be pulled backward, but there is no such law. A train is meant to be pulled from the front engine, not from the last car. You must understand this.

Firm belief in the center
Therefore, what you must know is that you must have a firm belief. You must have a firm belief in the center. If you have a firm belief that you will do this, ten years will not be a problem. I know you are going this way. But I do not speak of it even though I know. If you think your belief is the best, then I challenge you to prove it. Do not become a cheap imitation. Ultimately, what I am saying is, do not think about how you will live well or prosper. Because we were born as descendants of fallen ancestors, we should not think that by living a life of faith we will do well or receive blessings. Do not keep hoping for blessings. That is a mistaken thought. In a life of faith, we should think about how we can die well and how we can perish well.

Heaven has been working until now to destroy this satanic world. It was to destroy individuals of the satanic world, families of the satanic world, tribes of the satanic world, nations of the satanic world, and ultimately the entire satanic world.

Until today, the Unification Church has gone through so many trials and pains, but I am still fighting day and night to maintain a position where God can show compassion. 134   Requirements for a New Start  
The interdenominational movement and the Principle Study Group movement were peripheral movements for activities in the 1970s.  
The external influence through the activities of our Japanese members is good, but the internal elite personnel are a problem. In the future, we need 7,000 to 12,000 university graduates. If Christians come in, they can become personnel after just two months of training.  
To create human resources, economic issues follow. To carry out interdenominational movements, student movements, etc., substantial funds are needed. At least several tens of millions of won are necessary. If the required financial resources are supported, we can absorb existing churches as well.  
After Professor Seo Nam-dong's lecture at the Saemunan Church, the Unification Church became widely recognized as something that cannot be eliminated, and even groups that feel fear have emerged.  
The interest of existing church leaders in our interdenominational movement has increased. Therefore, we must actively develop activities against existing churches and student movements. Various resources will inevitably be needed here.  
Together with the current key personnel, we must cultivate a second generation of personnel to achieve our goals in the 1970s.  
Ideologically, we need to make it known nationwide that it must be the Unification Church; however, as I reiterate, this requires resources.  
Currently, we are in debt of about 100 million won due to air gun-related matters.  
In the 1980s, we must ensure that the sound of the song of unification can be heard anywhere in the world. To do so, we must think of sunset and night as enemies and run day and night.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, on this morning of the first Sunday of the last month of 1969, please grant us your mercy and love. Also, please allow our hearts to draw closer to yours at this time.  
Before you, the subject of high, precious, and holy grace, we, who are lowly, humble, and miserable, bow our heads like this, hoping to be embraced under the shadow of your heart.  
In the midst of such tranquility, let us feel your life’s pulse acting upon all our moving organs, and let us be able to perceive your living presence amidst the sound of that heartbeat. May we feel your call and the connection with you pulsating, and may we become those who desire to feel the holy image of our Father and become exceedingly holy.

<Words> People living on this earth cannot only lead happy lives.
We know that this is the case, and we are also experiencing it directly. Just as individuals are so, families are likewise, and nations and states are the same. Even when we look at the current state of the world, we understand that this is true. Therefore, today, all of humanity is living on a stage of life where we must navigate through conditions of misfortune. The history of the past has flowed in this way, the present is the same, and we know that the future history will also continue in such an environment.

As the central entity of all things, 

I

In such an environment, the issue lies with us individuals who possess a single life. Sadness begins and ends with the individual. This is the fate of us humans living in the present age.

The wounds of disgrace

A nation cannot resolve its own sadness. To resolve the sadness of such a nation, each citizen must seek some motivation and connection within themselves to address that sadness. Without this, the entire nation cannot escape from conditions of unhappiness or evil.

Even if we pursue happiness for the entire world, that happiness cannot come all at once centered around the whole. Before the happiness of the world is achieved, the happiness of each individual living in the world must first sprout on this earth. Therefore, as long as individual happiness does not bear fruit on this earth, it is impossible for the happiness of the world to be realized.

When we focus on these points, we come to realize how important our individual selves are today. We stand on the boundary line where we can be the source of happiness or the source of unhappiness. These individuals, that is, each of us, do not exist solely as individuals. Above me are my parents, below me are my children, and to my left and right are my siblings. Additionally, in front and behind me are my nation and humanity.

Then, when we consider how my single entity can become the central entity of this whole, we find that no matter how deep history is or how great the connections are, when it is outside of me, it has no relation to me. Countless nations scattered throughout the world, or countless humans, may appear to be happy, or numerous social phenomena in the present world may seem happy, but until that happiness is connected to me, it holds no meaning. Therefore, I must understand that my existence is not in a position distinct from the whole, but rather in a position that represents the whole.

Thus, in creating history, when I establish myself in a fresh form, a new history will be created. Also, in the pursuit of happiness historically, if I do not find my own fresh form, happiness or peace on this earth will have no relation to me. In this way, everything is connected around me, and we must recognize that everything is influenced by me.

The importance of my existence

So why is it that humans stand in such a position? It is because, before the absolute God, who is the foundation of all life and the center of the entire universe, humans are in the closest relative position. In other words, humans are positioned as the only object before the one and only absolute subject. Therefore, it is established that today, all conditions of happiness and unhappiness must be connected to my individual self, that is, to the fallen individual.

Thus, happiness can begin from a relative individual before the absolute subject, and truth can be formed, and freedom, hope, victory, or glory can sprout from there. Moreover, it does not end there. It can be the source of overall happiness and the center of all conditions of hope. Therefore, we must establish connections of happiness and hope throughout the world centered around such individuals. Only through such connections can a new world of happiness or hope appear on this earth. Therefore, unless the true self that can be the condition of all hope appears on this earth, no happiness will be related to oneself, and no wish will be related to oneself. It will simply pass by.

In the face of the flow of history, or in the life of humanity forming connections of life, the true happiness that can be left behind must inevitably appear at a point that can be in harmony with the absolute. Therefore, this "I" is the problem. There are 3 billion people in the world flowing through history. Among them, we must become the "I" that can stand in the position of a master. If God presents happiness to humanity, that happiness will begin through some center, and we must become that center so that happiness can start through us. We must long for that "I" that can initiate happiness from such a center.

The world is pursuing a single world, an ideal world, or happiness and goodness, which do not change depending on the time. When we become the center that can govern history and stand in the position that can move the fortunes of heaven and earth, from that point on, we will be able to live eternally with the eternal absolute. Living and dying can be done in accordance with the absolute. Therefore, all of humanity cannot help but wish to become such an "I."

The good person of today determines their position based on such a standard as a point. Depending on how far the distance is from that center, what the angle is, or what the direction is, it is decided whether one is a patriot before the nation, a great person before the world, or a sage before humanity.

Various ideologies that differ in direction from that one center are not what we desire. This is because there is a distance from the center we demand. We are in a position where we are distanced from that center and do not possess completeness. Therefore, we are seeking truth and happiness from a position where there is no distance from that center, which can be the origin of all that we desire. Such a place must inevitably exist.

Today, the position that can be the center of the individual cannot help but be the center of the family as well. Therefore, the family connected to such an individual, the society centered around that family, the nation centered around that society, and the world centered around that nation, that world is precisely the place of hope we must go to, the world of hope. Wouldn't that world be called Utopia or the paradise on earth?

When we consider from the perspective of humanity pursuing the highest realm of truth completed in the course of history, where would be the place God wants to go and stay centered around humanity? That place must be where such a center is established.

An important means to find such a place is religion. Religion is merely a means to find a path toward such a place. Therefore, we must carefully examine the relationship between religion and ourselves from that foundation.

Our destination

To wash away the wounds of disgrace

Everyone, today’s message title is the wounds of disgrace, right? The term disgrace (受辱) has come up; what is disgrace? It is shame, shame. What is this shame? It arises when one receives treatment that is not true despite being true. When one is treated as if they are not true despite being true, shame arises there, and when that shame and disgrace are truly recognized, it becomes disgrace. In other words, when truth is completely denied in its true position, the term disgrace arises. Thus, when one stands in a position from which they cannot escape that state, it becomes infinite suffering and infinite unhappiness.

To illustrate again, a child who is a devoted son before their parents fulfills the duty of a devoted son to the extent that the parents are pleased, and thus the parents and child can be completely united. That person is a devoted son. However, when such a devoted son is attacked as if he is not a devoted son, and is placed in a position where he must return to the position of a true devoted son, it becomes the utmost disgrace. If the value of a devoted son united with their parents holds a value of millions, then the wounds of disgrace for the person in a disgraceful position are equally deep.

If one wishes to wash that away, what must be done? They must rise to a higher position. What happens when one rises to that higher position? A head arises in the heart of the child, and a head arises in the heart of the parents. A boundary line between the two heads is formed. Moreover, the positions of those two boundary lines appear differently. As the positions of the two boundary lines gradually become distant, if left alone, they will eventually separate forever.

So how can we unify these boundary lines? It is not enough to simply unify the boundary lines. We must seek a way to cross that boundary line after unifying it. Without doing so, it will not be possible to return to the original state. Isn't that right?

If a devoted son has caused sorrow in the heart of the parents, to remove that sorrow from the parents, the standards of devotion that have been held until now will not suffice. What has been done until now will not do. The standards of devotion that have been believed until now must be discerned with new eyes. One must critically evaluate the standards of devotion that have been believed until now. It is not enough to remain in the position of devotion with the standards that still have conditions for criticism and discernment. One must exceed those standards of devotion. Only then can the wounds of disgrace suffered by the parents be washed away.

The same applies to the relationship between a ruler and loyal subjects in a nation. In the relationship between a king and a loyal subject, when the subject has been praised in a position where they are told, "You are my loyal subject. You are our glory, and our relationship can be eternally recorded in history," but then suddenly appears as a traitor, how great would the wound be for that king? To restore the position of a loyal subject from the past, one must demonstrate loyalty hundreds of times greater and establish the duty of loyalty thousands of times greater than before. Yet, even then, it is difficult to turn the heart of the king. Even if one shows loyalty a thousand times greater than before, it is difficult to turn the heart of the king that has been wounded. The wounds that have formed in the heart of the king cannot be remedied. The king will not forget that even after a thousand years. The stronger the trust and hope in that subject, the greater the pain felt in proportion to that. The king will always carry that painful heart. Therefore, without showing loyalty thousands or millions of times greater to heal that painful heart of the king and wash away the wounds of disgrace suffered by the king, there is no way to restore the position of a loyal subject from the past.

If you have received the teaching from your parents that you must do this even if it means dying, then despite having fallen, you must break away from the fallen environment and say, "I will live like this," and struggle to live that way. The more you are pressured by that environment, the closer you will become to your parents. This is an indirect operation that evokes God's heart. This operation is the most excellent method to receive God's compassion.

Isn't that the case in the world as well? When a child makes a mistake, elders in the neighborhood come forward and say, "I did the same when I was young," providing evidence of forgiveness. Then the parents have no choice but to forgive. Even if the child has fallen, if they sincerely repent in their heart and struggle to keep the commands of their parents, even when faced with thousands of fallen people trying to pull them down, they must struggle to keep the commands of their parents. Thus, even if they are wounded and die while trying to keep those commands, when they finally reach that position, God will once again show compassion as a parent. It is in such a position that we can receive God's compassion. This is the fastest path.

In other words, we must be able to stand up for heaven, advocate for goodness on behalf of heaven, confront Satan on behalf of heaven, and boldly declare before Satan, "Go ahead and do what you want. No matter what you do, I cannot do that." We must be able to stand in that position. It is not about boasting to God, "I am Your son," but rather saying to Satan, "Try to do again the actions that have caused me countless unjust wounds against God." We must be able to rise up through the process governed by Satan and stand confidently. Only by standing in such a position can we receive God's love. In any other way, we cannot receive God's love even if we stand on heaven's side. No matter how much we strive centered on heaven, we cannot do it alone.

The common path that fallen humans must take

That is why, just because those on the path of virtue have understood such connections, it does not mean that a perfect connection is established. So what must be done to establish that connection? One must inevitably enter the world of enemies and go through the process of suffering disgrace. Otherwise, the connection cannot be made. That is the history of the providence of restoration. The place of restoration is the place of death.

The starting point of the fall was when I sought the worth of life centered on my own desires. Therefore, the path of resurrection opens up from the moment one resolves to seek the place of death.

That is why true religion must go beyond the hill of death. This death is not dying in the loving hands of God. It is not dying in front of parents, peers, neighbors, relatives, or even one’s nation. It means dying in front of those who are distant from me and oppose my nation. When one enters such a world of opposition and dies in a position of opposition, God, who has been wounded before the world, will show compassion for that person.

The true path of filial piety is not merely staying within the realm of heaven and believing and following heaven. You must understand that you must enter the world of opposition and be recognized as a filial child there and return. This is the only fastest path.

Thus, even Jesus, when praying in the Garden of Gethsemane at the end, said, "Abba Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as You will." Here, my will is to live, and the Father's will is to die. If He is to create a filial child and a loyal son, He should have granted the son’s wish, but why did God set up an opposing will that drove Jesus away?
To enter a position similar to that of the ancestors of humanity who betrayed you, both God must turn away from him and Satan must enter a position of betrayal. Since Satan has also betrayed and Heaven has likewise betrayed, if God were to show compassion, Satan would also have to show compassion. Thus, God was driven away, and that became the motive for a new history.

Until just before Jesus' fate, Satan was in a position of great power, but after Jesus died, he had to bow his head. Therefore, God takes a position opposite to Satan and walks this path. As a result, a new history began to unfold, with the rise of a new commandment and the motive for a new beginning, which is why today Christianity has formed a global cultural sphere.

In other words, the fallen sons and daughters who caused God sorrow, that is, the sons and daughters whom Satan led and delighted in, have died. The sons and daughters who were used by Satan and caused despair to God have died.

However, now that God's wish has begun, the path that Satan hoped for has turned into despair. Therefore, it is said that those who wish to die will live, and those who wish to live will die. This is a saying that transcends a thousand miles. Here, the question arises whether this path is not a common path that fallen humanity must take.

When will the wounds of disgrace disappear? If a son or daughter appears who can step over the history trampled by the enemy and rise up against it, mobilizing the entirety of the past, present, and future to attack, God will be liberated from the day of disgrace. Wouldn't that be the case?

How can we erase the wounds of disgrace that God has suffered?

Now, the 1960s, which we should be grateful for before the Father, is disappearing before us. We are in the process of stepping on the end of the 1960s and welcoming the new beginning of the 1970s. Today is December 14, 1969, and there are only 17 days left in the 1960s. During this period, we must once again clarify ourselves. 

We have come to realize that the past ten years, during which we have responded to the Father's call and taken on the historical destiny, are different from today’s point. When we look at ourselves before entering the Unification Church and after entering it, if reality is criticized by the past, that is shameful, it is a descent, and it is a distance from that world. We must realize that we are not a lost sheep but are within the flock of ninety-nine sheep. We must understand that we are in such a position. 

Since we are talking about our current values, our appearance in front of the will today should have developed compared to the past, but if it has not and has instead regressed, that is a pitiful position. We must rise again from here. We must once again hold onto the Father’s garment and delve into the deep roots of the Father’s heart. 

"My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?" In the final scene, when God turned His face away and avoided Jesus' death, just as Jesus said, "Abba Father, receive my life," the mission to conclude the final judgment lies within the Unification Church. The process of the cross of the Unification Church remains here. A moment when the Unification Church can be newly resurrected is approaching us. 

We must understand the situation of Jesus, who, while sharing bread at the Last Supper with the twelve disciples, felt sorrow knowing that there was an enemy present. We must not stand in the same position as that enemy. We must stand in a position where even the enemy praises the glory of victory and submits. All creation must see this and praise God as the glorious, joyful God. We must prepare our victory, our mouth, our cells, so that we can sing and dance before the Father in a glorious form. 

We must achieve resurrection not by dying but by living. We must not carry the grievances of the enemy in death but rather resolve those grievances while living, for that is the path of unity. Thus, we have come to this point, even in the position of being treated as enemies. 

When we lift our heads, we see that there is one threshold left to cross. When we step over this threshold, a bright world will be prepared before us. Let us face the barriers of trials we encounter at this present moment and overcome them vigorously. We must know for certain that when we confront with a power greater than death, we will be victorious. May this time allow us to reaffirm such a resolution. 

Now we have welcomed the Sabbath with only three weeks remaining until today. Starting from today, we earnestly hope and wish that we can make new resolutions in the remaining period and become your children who can welcome the 1970s. 

With today’s message, we have responsibilities to carry out, to decide and implement new historical tasks. We must gladly accept that path and mission and head towards the second indemnity settlement. Let us clear away the clouds of heart that have caused the Father to feel sorrow until now, shake off our shameful posture, and move towards tomorrow's hope. May we become a victorious figure who can stand before the nation and the world in a position where the Father’s wishes are fulfilled, where the Father agrees, and where we receive the Father’s joyful welcome in His history. 

Please remember the children scattered across the nation and the world. Remember your children fighting in Japan, and may our plans centered around the great assembly in Asia next year progress rapidly under the protection of your will. May we become your children who can start vigorously to prepare for tomorrow's victory with the conviction of overcoming, along with today’s words. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 

The Lord of the Harvest
Matthew 19:28-30
<Prayer (I)> Father, today is December 14, 1969, the second Sabbath of this month. Father, it has been over 20 years since the words of unification have appeared on this earth and the path of unification has begun. 
We must not forget the time when you searched for an individual who could convey your sorrowful circumstances behind countless nations, holding the will of restoration that no one else knew. 

Since the day Abel was killed by Cain, sorrow has filled the heavens and the earth, and as we trace the path of restoration, how can we comfort the Father, who has become so humble? After working for 1,600 years through ten generations since Adam, you sent Noah to this earth and earnestly asked him to fulfill your wishes. How anxious were you during those tedious 120 years, waiting for that time to come? How earnest was your heart in wanting to ask Noah? How pitiful and how difficult was the situation of the Father, who could not relax and ask on any given day? 

The family of Noah was the wish of heaven, a family that was to be harvested as the fruit of heaven's labor, but due to Ham's mistake, the path of Ham was extended unexpectedly, and you had to look forward to the time of Abraham. Indeed, the path of the Father was a pitiful path. 

When you called Abraham out of the family of Terah in Ur of the Chaldeans, you were in an extremely pitiful position. When we think about the miserable circumstances and content of the Father, who had to take that son out of a family he loved dearly, we recall once again how much the consequences of the fall of our human ancestors have caused you pain throughout the twists and turns of history. 

We want to understand the heart of the Father when you chose Abraham, and we want to be young in the earnest heart you had towards Abraham. Therefore, may we become sons and daughters who can be called in place of Abraham before you, who come to visit us at this time. 

How pitiful must the Father have felt to ask Abraham to leave his beloved hometown and relatives and to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, transcending all circumstances? Here, we glimpse the fact that the Father’s situation cannot be resolved without driving beloved children into a pitiful position, and that the Father cannot connect with His situation and relationships without leading beloved children through a path of misery. 

Abraham left Ur of the Chaldeans. His path, which followed heaven while abandoning everything, was a lonely path. It was a sorrowful path. It was the path of a wanderer. He had to go without receiving help from anyone, and even though he wanted to serve heaven, he was in the position of a traveler, so he could only serve heaven in his heart. When we reflect on the path of Abraham, we realize how pitiful the steps of a believer can be. 

Thus, we come to feel how anxious the Father was until Jacob established the foundation of heaven’s victory. Until then, there was no one who could establish the Father’s wishes. Looking at the earth, there was only the land of darkness, and looking at countless humanity, there were only the children of the enemy. Looking at this world, it was a distant world of darkness where one could not connect with heaven. 

However, centered on the descendants of Abraham, through Isaac and Jacob, the day came when the will of heaven was laid on this earth, and from that day, his descendants had to become wanderers who had to start to establish the nation of Israel centered on Jacob’s family. How pitiful was that path? They were crowded everywhere they went. They suffered injustice everywhere they went. They had to pioneer a lonely path that could only communicate with heaven, where no one on this earth could listen to their circumstances or advice. 

From the day Jacob went to Egypt with his 70 family members, the Israelite nation lived in misery for 400 long years. That nation could not escape from the hands of the enemy. They could not escape from the whip of the enemy. 

In the midst of this, the Father raised Moses, who had a heart longing for heaven, a heart loving heaven, a heart pursuing the welfare of Israel, and a burning patriotism. Thus, after hearing the Father’s command to encourage and lead the Israelite nation, Moses also had to stand in a fate where he could not help but hold onto the Israelite nation alone, abandoning everything. 

As we trace the 4,000 years of history up to the time of Jesus through the path of Moses, how sorrowful you must have been, Father! The remnants who survived amidst the ridicule, persecution, and death at the hands of enemies had to pioneer a path that could restore the altar of Israel and relieve the Father’s sorrowful circumstances. Despite having that responsibility left, the Israelite nation hesitated. 

They hoped for the glory of heaven before taking on such responsibilities. They demanded only the glory they were to receive without passing through the gate of the cross they were to bear. That is why we know they lost the coming Jesus. 

Due to this sad event, Christianity has come out over the past 2,000 years with the crisis of death ahead. While developing globally, how much blood did the Father pay in that process, and how much sorrow, loneliness, and resentment did He endure? When we think about what the fruits of Christianity, which paid that price, truly were, we must understand that heaven cannot help but despair and cannot help but lose hope at this present moment. 

At such a time, your children gathered here have already stepped onto a different path. They have chosen a lonely path. They have stepped forward knowing the sorrowful circumstances of heaven. If that is the case, have we truly understood heaven? Have we truly understood the Father’s situation? If we have understood, we must realize once again that those who know this cannot be in this state. 

Father, please look down upon your children gathered here today! When we ask again whose footsteps the Father has come to find, there must be sons and daughters who realize that it is the footsteps of the Father coming to find themselves. At this time, may we be your children who can realize such things, Father, we earnestly hope and wish. 

Now the 1960s are fading away. With only 17 days left in the 1960s, it has been a year of sorrow, a year of resentment, a year of sadness, a year of pain, a year of misery, and a year of injustice. Having spent these ten years, we must ask ourselves whether we have truly become the fruit of heaven harvested as a result of ten years of labor.
When I think of the division, I discover that I am ashamed before Heaven. Here, I earnestly hope and desire to be allowed to realize that we must repent before Heaven once again. We are humans who could not be born with You, who cannot live with You, and who cannot die with You. However, You have taught us the way to live with You, and for that, we must give thanks a million times for Your grace. I realize that even if I offer this body as a living sacrifice before You, it is still insufficient, and I feel once again that our appearances are dirty to present before You.

Therefore, we are ashamed to present this body before You, covering and hiding it, worrying about how to conceal this appearance, as we are individual beings who should appear before You. Yet, despite this, we have been so arrogant before You. We have been so proud before You. And yet, we appeared with the boldness to directly inform You to accept this appearance, saying, "I am Your son and daughter."

Father, please have compassion on us. We are a group of sinners born in the world of sin, destined to fall. However, because You have extended the hand of salvation that allows us to dwell with You, we have gathered here in Your holy sanctuary with the grace to dwell with You. 

Father, the path You must take is the path of a wanderer that must go through individuals, families, nations, and the world. There must be true children here who can keep that path and become dutiful sons and daughters before You, so I earnestly hope and desire that You will look down upon us.

I also ask that You fully preside over this time today, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
