<Words> The title of the message I wish to deliver today is "The Lord of the Harvest." I will speak briefly on this title.  
The Absolute Being and Myself Viewed Through Motive and Result  
There are many people gathered here, and every existence has a motive that must arise. There cannot be a reality that transcends the content of that motive. In other words, as beings of result, we cannot deny that we are necessarily connected to the motive. When you look at yourselves, you can clearly observe what your parents must have looked like based on your appearance and what your physique must have been like based on your body.  
Just as individuals are, this world of results is a world of miserable outcomes, so the world that causes this must also be miserable.  
We know that this world cannot be the place of peace we envision or the place of happiness we desire. When we acknowledge that this is a world of results, there must necessarily be a motive. There cannot be a result that transcends the starting point of any motive, so it must be that the motive also carries such miserable content. This is a simple matter that can be understood through common sense.  
From this perspective, whether we look at ourselves, our families, or the world, it is undeniable that this result is flawed. Therefore, it is unnecessary to say that the starting point of our human ancestors was not one that could sing of happiness, nor could it be a central being that could portray a glorious posture before all creation, immersed in ideals. Thus, we arrive at the conclusion that we cannot help but pursue the fallen ancestors of humanity as spoken of in religion.  
If we pursue the motives that can be the foundation of humanity, we will find the ancestors of humanity. Speaking from the perspective of the Bible, there would be Adam and Eve. However, since Adam and Eve are also beings of result, we must trace back beyond them. In doing so, we will be able to acknowledge the existence of the Absolute Being.  
Human beings possess all dominion over creation. When we consider your heart's actions or your conscious faculties, we find that humans are intricately made. If we develop our observational abilities in one direction, we can become subjective beings capable of observing even to the ends of the earth.  
The God who created such humans is not a God who can be confined within our thoughts. He is a being that cannot be defined by our thoughts or measured by any standard. Therefore, as we pursue Him, the concept of the Absolute Being will automatically arise. When we consider the content of the creation of heaven and earth, if we acknowledge that we were created, then there must also be a Creator.  
If the human ancestors became the motive for producing results like those we see today, what kind of being would the God who could be the origin of humanity be? Could the one who created this world, which is imperfect, requiring cultivation and correction, truly be the Absolute Being? It cannot be so.  
When we look at the structure of the human body, it is a realm of mystery. It is composed of mystery itself, more than any other existence. If there is an Absolute Being who has connected all the elements of mystery to create the one life form known as humanity, He must undoubtedly be the master of infinite power.  
Then, could that being, who is the source of all existence, also be flawed? If He could be flawed, then ideals, happiness, hope, and peace could not exist in the human world. Such things would merely be dreams. If it began with something that could be flawed, and that became the result, leading to an end, then the conclusion that heaven does not exist would automatically arise.  
However, the inclinations of our human hearts seek a perfect origin beyond the imperfect origin. This transcends the historical environment and the strong waves of the times, and it has been pulsating within our hearts until now. When we see that the source of that power and the stimulus of that power remain, we must conclude that the original basis, or essence, or causal existence that can be the subject of that power must be an absolute being. Humans are always seeking something new, something ideal, something peaceful and happy through that direction of the heart.  
How did the pursuit of another result come to be? The origin of such a motive does not directly relate to our humanity or our living environment, nor does it connect with the global environment, but it has established a connection deep within the valleys of our hearts. This has stimulated the development of a new era of history and a new era of culture.  
The Source of the Power that Stimulates the Human Heart  
Therefore, in the future, the world we must pursue is one world. That world and humanity must become a world beyond the current world and a humanity beyond the current humanity. The nation that constitutes that world must become a nation that is more than the many nations that have existed until now, gathered together. Thus, there must arise a sovereignty that can replace many sovereigns, a sovereignty that can represent the numerous sovereigns that have appeared throughout history. A people must emerge who can love the world with a love greater than that which many citizens have had for their own countries. Humans are pursuing such things.  
The content of the motive that can bring this about has not yet disappeared from the foundation of our hearts today, and it is presented as a stimulating motive that directs us towards tomorrow. So where does this fact originate? There is a source that allows this to happen.  
Everyone, power comes from the interaction between the subject and the object. All the stimulating sensations you feel cannot be felt alone. They must be felt through the conditions of the object. You feel through the action of the object's power. Action is power, and power cannot arise without a subject and an object.  
The action of our human conscience, which urges us for the hope of tomorrow, takes tomorrow as a stage of hope, and seeks to pursue a more valuable personality, where does all this power come from? It must come from a place where there is a relationship between the subject and the object. Without that, such actions of power do not occur. This is also true in chemical reactions. If the elements of the subject and the object are not each equipped, they will absolutely not act. There is no action that results in loss.  
When you come to this place of the Unification Church, did you come to suffer a loss? Absolutely not. You must have come seeking something that can be a plus for yourself through a relationship with some subject and object. In both physical and chemical actions, there can be no action that results in loss.  
From this perspective, all beings are inclined to seek a place that can be beneficial to themselves, a place of greater value, a place that can shine more brightly; they do not act to incur loss. When you say you are going to Myeongdong, do you say, "I am going to Myeongdong to lose a few tens of won today"? No one would say that. The purpose pursued by all beings is to seek conditions that can be beneficial to them, centered on the relationship between subject and object.  
All human heart actions are the same. The reality of the world we live in is such, and the actions occurring in the human heart must also have a subject. We do not know what that subject is, but it exists. That power cannot act alone. Therefore, even within my individual self, there is an exchange between subject and object. When the subject and object exchange, there is joy. Happiness comes, love sprouts, and hope sprouts.  
From this perspective, if we pursue the actions of our hearts, there must be a being that serves as the essence of the heart. Since my resultant self cannot exist beyond the original being, I must acknowledge a perfect plus form that can be the source of all existence. Then, what kind of being is that? The name of that being does not matter. However, that being is the absolute subject, the highest being that cannot be surpassed by anyone, and a central being that does not permit relative conditions.  
The Purpose of God's Creation of Heaven and Earth  
Your hearts seek a tomorrow that is better and happier than today. This means pursuing even more precious results, seeking even more precious values. So what is the end of that pursuit? Is it a world of conflict? No, it is not.  
What is the end of the world that the Absolute Being, the absolute protagonist who created heaven and earth, desires? It is a world that can be a sovereign nation, a world that can possess a national identity, a world that can be a garden, a foundation of sovereignty. That is what is required. <Words> Today, I will speak for a moment on the title "The Path of Restoration We Must Take."

There are countless people living on this land. There are also numerous ethnicities and many nations. Although we humans do not know, when we look at individuals or a nation, we must understand that they stand on the foundation of paying the price of restoration centered on God.

Some people live well, while others do not. Some nations boast of being advanced countries with a sense of authority, while others struggle from the position of developing countries. When we look at the reality of the world in this way, there are things that may appear good and things that may appear bad. It is not just about size; we know that such connections revolve around us from all directions—front and back, left and right, up and down.

The Backdrop of Wealthy and Poor Nations
We can see that wealthy nations stand on the foundation of having paid a corresponding price. By examining the history of that nation, we can understand why they are wealthy. Likewise, we can glimpse the fact that poor nations have the motives for their poverty behind them.

When we look at it this way, whether it is an individual or a nation, it is not the case that they have lived well from the past to the present. Even large nations had to make decisions at the crossroads of life and death, centered around miserable content, in order to become wealthy nations. We must recognize that they have come through many historical events. And those events were not resolved because individuals were capable, but because the people and the nation united and put their entire fate on the line to resolve them. In resolving national emergencies, the entire upper and lower, left and right must unite and go through the process of overcoming crises, which brings about continuous results of development, allowing that nation to establish itself as an advanced country today.

On the other hand, when we look at backward nations, we see that there is no innovative content that has vigorously overcome crises for a hopeful tomorrow behind them. They neglected to risk their lives to overcome crises and did not take responsibility for it. The entire nation, the upper and lower, left and right, could not move to overcome such crises. We must understand that the less a nation has acted in unified action, the more it cannot avoid being a developing country. History has unfolded this way.

The Process of Struggle Necessary for Success
If this is true for a nation's history, it is the same for individuals. When we consider what we will leave behind in the new historical era that is approaching, we can see that the factors determining that content lie not in the surrounding environment but within ourselves. This fact can be observed in both advanced and developing countries throughout history.

The same applies to our individual destinies. Whether a person succeeds in their time or not, or whether they encounter a glorious era or leave behind a sorrowful and lamentable life, can be understood by looking at the process of how they live their lives. It depends on how much they can align with the historical direction and the direction of heavenly fortune from the moment they are born, or whether they have faced the events that come to them head-on with a heart that seeks the future beyond their own life.

The greater the wish and purpose, the greater the struggle required. The process of struggle cannot be absent. Struggle itself is not something everyone desires. However, without struggle, the goals they desire cannot be achieved. This is an absolute fact.

In a rapidly changing reality, one cannot seek a new purpose within that environment. They must overcome the existing reality. To expand a new foundation for living, one must establish the two characters of revolution regarding their own environment and go through the path of struggle. This is the path that those who seek their purpose must inevitably take. While everyone may welcome success at the point of results, no one welcomes the past that led to success, nor the process of achieving it. The days leading up to success were likely a series of historical days that made one shudder and want to give up. This is true for one's parents, peers, friends, children, and spouses.

The past itself was a matter of bloody struggle. Without overcoming this process of conflicting extremes, one cannot fulfill their purpose. This is true for a lifetime and also for a single day. As one starts their day in the morning, they may hope that today will be a meaningful day, but it is not simple for that day to bear the results of the meaningful day they long for. Those who face such a complicated day and pass it simply become simple people. We must not live our lives in a way that is similar to those who have such a perspective.

When we look at an individual's life or even at countries that claim to be advanced today, we can see that there is a long path of struggle behind them. The value of existence for that individual or nation is determined by the price paid to break free from an environment that must inevitably retreat.

What Path Has the Unification Church Walked?
In this light, what path has our Unification Church walked? As we stand before the new restoration providence era of the 1970s, I cannot help but ask this question. Moreover, do we have the confidence that we will not fall or perish here? We will not fall or perish. We can stand even more firmly. We can say that we have the confidence to pay a greater price. If you carry such confidence, you will not become one of those who disappear in the sorrow of this era.

Those who have put brakes on us and imposed restrictions will inevitably find themselves in the position of losers because of us. If we have such awareness and confidence while facing this reality, we cannot fail. Even if my hands are empty and my body is bare, there is hope for tomorrow.

Then, when I look at myself as a member of the Unification Church, what price have I paid for the church? Therefore, what we are facing now is temporary, and what is to come is eternal. If someone has truly grasped this fact, they will feel the infinite difference between that value and themselves. The question is how confidently, meaningfully, and valuably can one pay the price compared to this? When we consider this question, we must reflect on how each of you sitting here today has done. 

If all the factors of development in the historical era have been so, and if the fate of this era's nation, which accompanies the eternal fate of history, is determined by the standard of the price paid, is the remaining period of restoration in this Unification Church unfortunate? No, it is not. We must not shy away from this heart; rather, we must become a nation that can joyfully surpass this, not only for our own generation but also for the second and third generations. If there is such a nation or such a person, that nation and that person will not perish.
you must first pay the price. The path of restoration is not an easy one; it requires sacrifice and commitment.

In conclusion, the path of restoration is a journey that requires dedication, sacrifice, and unity. It is a journey that we must undertake together, with a shared vision and a commitment to creating a better world for ourselves and for those who will come after us. Let us embrace this challenge and move forward with courage and determination.

12) The final moment  
<Prayer> Father, today is the last Sabbath of the 1960s.  
The sad history of the 1960s, in which You crossed over countless nations to find this Korean Peninsula and the Korean people, is about to pass.  
Until now, many children have spent holy Sabbaths. Now, as we long for Your infinite love and grace in our hearts, we have been pioneering the path of restoration.

Father, as you reflect on the past at this moment, please forget the sorrowful past. Please let go of the burdens of this unfortunate nation. I hope you will forget all the wrongs this nation has committed against you.

When the children of unification appeared before this nation as the heavenly messengers, this nation should have exalted your beloved sons and daughters, praised your supremacy, and gathered their hearts to worship you. Yet, they raised a rebellion against you. Please forgive their past mistakes. The children who stood at the forefront have walked a lonely path that no one knows. Some have stood in places of oppression, some have been exiled, and some have walked this path even in the position of being the body of English. However, let them realize that the events that occurred during this process should not remain as memories filled with sorrow. And if this nation has wronged them, I pray for your forgiveness.

The children of unification, who have carried the Abel-like mission, must restore their Cain-like brothers, and furthermore, it is our destiny to restore Cain's families, tribes, nations, and the world. Therefore, just as we must accept personal arrows of blame, persecution at home, and trials in society, we have meditated on you as if we were the guilty ones, calling upon you in the past... We realized that we should not look upon this nation with sorrow in our hearts, along with your sorrow. We understood that we must open our hearts and not treat even our enemies as enemies but with love, and we must have compassion for our Cain-like brothers.

Who would have known that Joseph would meet his eleven brothers again in the land of Egypt? Even when standing in a sorrowful and lonely place, if we become supporters of truth and stand by the side of truth, enduring until the end, we have learned through history that the Cain-like brothers who persecuted us will surely surrender. That is why we have endured for a long time.

Father, please love the Republic of Korea now, and love the many religions that guide the spiritual world of this nation and people. Father, please break all the arrows of evil that have flown toward us until now. We do not regard them as enemies, so we earnestly hope you will forgive them.

Your path is good, and when we think that the results of goodness must appear, we know that forgiveness and tolerance must fundamentally manifest. Since you are the essence of goodness, we earnestly wish that you would forgive the past when many religious people in this country persecuted the children of unification with your infinite love and tolerance.

Although we have knocked on the door of unification, some have fallen away due to loneliness because we could not meet even one person to comfort us on the path of persecution and tears. We also know that many people walking this path are weary. 

We understand that this falling away and weariness is due more to an inadequate environment than to our own faults. Therefore, when we think of those who are bowing their heads and asking for forgiveness toward you on the streets or in their situations today, we feel an unbearable resentment to relieve the heart of the Father who bears grudges, but when we think of the path of your merciful restoration that has come to find the children of the enemy, we know that we cannot help but bless them again with tears in our eyes. We earnestly hope you will forgive them, the pitiful group that has betrayed and turned against you, and remember them again.

I must go beyond the thirty million people of the Republic of Korea to the world, which is why I give gifts to the church. After completing that history of liberation, after giving to the thirty million people, what will we do? We must gather those who opposed us. It is a matter of time. Since it must be given anyway, why should we harbor resentment and think bitterly while we should be giving? When giving, we should do so with a big heart and share everything. Isn’t that so? It is a matter of time.

The Unification Church is currently doing such work. To do such work, the Unification Church alone is not enough. We must unite with established churches. We must influence general religions by uniting Christianity. Thus, we must influence the thirty million people. We must connect from the Republic of Korea to Japan, Asia, and the world. Right now, we are doing that work.

Korea and Japan were enemies in the past. It was a historically enmity-laden nation where one could not even think of marrying due to the deep-seated hatred. However, that is no longer a problem. Now we must become the subject and object and spread the unified front. We must establish God's love between Korea and Japan. God's love is stronger than national love. It transcends any historical love, so that love surpasses nations. We aim to start vigorously centered around the 1970s, which is capable of executing such a tremendous task.

The Victorious Unified Front is to be united centered on God's love.
You must spread the victorious unified front starting from the individual. The victorious unified front is to be united centered on God's love. When the heart and body become one centered on the individual, God dwells there. When God dwells in the place where giving and taking occurs, reproduction must take place. If God does not dwell there, reproduction cannot occur. That is the principle of creation. Everything was created motivated by God's love, so without God, reproduction cannot happen. When giving and taking occurs, God dwells there, and reproduction takes place.

This unified front must be spread from the individual to the family, clan, nation, and world. Currently, our Unification Church has reached a position where it can seek the nation centered on the tribe. Now, the Unification Church has entered an era where it can influence the tribe and the nation. The global situation is fully prepared and has come to our doorstep. Now, when we peel off just one layer, we will soar. Just as Apollo 11, launched from Cape Kennedy, ignited its tail and took off, we too must head toward the time when we can do the same. We must not go and return without achieving our goals.

The issue lies in whether the recognition of my will is stronger than the recognition of my heart and body, or whether it is weaker. A strong magnet, once attached, does not easily detach, just as your hearts must be strongly united with the will. Thus, you must long for God alone, and...
You must have a thorough and unwavering mindset that says you live only for the Lord. If you have such a mindset, even if your body is broken and disappears, you will still remain. What does it mean when Jesus said, "It is finished" as He died? It means that, centered on that mindset, the purpose that must be achieved in the relative world has been spiritually fulfilled. However, that spirit is faint among you.

To achieve this, you must go through all the indemnity conditions. This cannot be done one-on-one. Therefore, you must set indemnity conditions and go through all of them. In other words, to expand the victorious unified front, you must go through the indemnity process centered on the Word. To do this, you must establish the relationship between subject and object starting from the individual, and expand it to the family, clan, tribe, nation, and state.

The way of the good is to sacrifice the small for the sake of the great. Is the family not greater than the individual? Therefore, the destination that the individual must reach is the family. The place that single men and women must go is the family that will be formed through marriage. The destination for men and women is the family. And what the family must seek is children. When children are born, siblings emerge, and from there, the tribe emerges.

The individual's purpose is the family, and the family's purpose is children. And from those children, the tribe is organized. After the tribe is organized, such tribes come together to form a nation. Thus, the nation is established. That nation is formed centered on you. Speaking in today's democratic terms, the president is like the representative of all the people. That is why it is said that the sovereignty of democracy lies with the people. 

When such a nation is established, the president becomes the elder brother of our family, and what is there to be jealous of when that elder brother works on my behalf? If the elder brother becomes a doctor, would I be jealous of the elder brother who used to hit me in the past? Wouldn't the father be happy, the mother be happy, and the siblings be happy?

Therefore, you must establish the family that the individual desires and the children that the family desires. Thus, you must restore the family expectation. When such restored families come together, what happens? They become tribes, nations, and states. Tribes, nations, and the world are all expanded families. 

If you create a family that can serve as a model and establish it as a global family, from there, 3 billion people can emerge, and even 360 billion people can emerge.

Heaven is not established elsewhere. It is established in the family. Before there can be a nation, there must be a tribe, and before there can be a tribe, there must be a family. Can there be a nation without a family? Yet, Christians say they believe in Jesus and want to go to heaven. Can a widower go to heaven alone? Jesus, being a widower, has not been able to enter heaven and has been waiting in paradise for 2,000 years. He is waiting for a bride.

Why does a husband cry when his wife dies? Because the path to obtaining the third purpose, children, has been broken. If that cannot be achieved, he can only collapse. He has no choice but to die. So, he has no choice but to cry. In electricity, there are positive (+) and negative (-) charges, and if one of these is lost, the other cannot function at all. The path of a person is the same.

That is why men and women must marry, establish families, and have children. Even if a family is established, that family cannot live alone. Relatives from that household, such as uncles and cousins, are needed. Is there anyone who, when asked if they need relatives, would say, "I don't need relatives. I like living alone"? Would anyone wish that all the citizens of the Republic of Korea were just ten people? Have you seen such a person? Chinese people boast that their population is 750 million, right? 

How to unify body and mind is the urgent priority. To become a true son or daughter of God, one must become a global person. One must be able to say, "This universe is mine." To do this, one must clear away all the barriers and fences that block the way and declare that the world is mine, to the point where people can say, "That's right." But what is the reality? There are many borders between countries, different cultural spheres, and different languages. It is all mixed up. So, this must be cleaned up. 

Thus, we must create a common language and live together, work together, and follow a single plan. If a plan is made to dig up Baekdu Mountain, everyone must take off their shirts and grab shovels. Are we, Unification Church members, like that? "Yes." If the teacher says to do it, do you have the confidence to do it? "Yes." Really? "Yes." Would you even want to dig up the graves of the parents of someone who opposes our Unification Church? "Yes."

Where is the victorious unified front? I am not saying that I want to become the president of the Republic of Korea. Do not misunderstand. Those who have misunderstood the teacher's words are saying all sorts of things. They say that the Unification Church is trying to overturn the current regime by expanding the unified front. What would be the point of overturning the tiny Republic of Korea? If you have such thoughts, should you not think about overturning Asia instead of thinking about the trivial current regime?

The victory activities I am currently engaged in will involve Japan, and this work is also being done in China, and China will also be involved. Just wait and see whether they get involved or not. Japan is already getting involved. Despite this situation, established Christians are saying that the Unification Church will fail, and Unification Church members are saying that they are dancing naked and talking about how terrible the leader is. Do you think that will make them disappear?

Victorious unified front, everyone, can you repeat after me? (Repeats) Where is the starting point of this victorious unified front? "Individual." How do you unify the body and mind of the individual? This is the issue. Those who are willing to follow the will even at the cost of their own lives are the true brave ones who have stepped forward to expand the unified front.

It is these men and women with such a mindset who meet and receive blessings. However, when you look at yourselves, you are two people, one heart and one body. These two are always fighting. When a man and a woman divided into body and mind come together, they become four people. Would it be happy if these four are fighting? It cannot be happy. If there are ten people, how many does that make? It becomes twenty. What happens when twenty people are fighting? The reason why families in the world tend to establish separate households is also here. When relatives live together, women say, "Honey, if my younger sibling doesn't bring in any household goods, we won't be able to survive." So, they separate.

The way to find refuge from fighting is only through separation. These days, in countries like America, there are men who say they do not need women. Men live alone in hotels. They sit in hotel rooms, smoking cigarettes or wandering the streets at night, and then come back to spend the night. It is complicated enough for two people to live together, so there is no reason to gather four people. When two people sit together, it is complicated. Isn't that so? If the mind and body of two people cannot become one and are fighting, how complicated would it be with four people? Therefore, they become burdensome and do not want to marry. 

American women seem to have a strong fate. They look very unpleasant. So, there are many widows. Korean women do not need to envy them. Who would they live with? Our Unification Church youth would probably say they dislike such women. I don't know if they would like them if I told them to. (Laughter)

What do you think? Is it better to be in the same room with someone whose heart matches yours, or with someone whose heart does not match yours? "With someone whose heart matches." That's right. It is good to be in the same room with those whose hearts match. But how about yourselves? Do your hearts and bodies match well? They do not match, do they? When will you make them one? This is the issue. This struggle has been woven into history, and many saints and wise people have died fighting this struggle. What is life? Is there a God? Many have died while fighting such struggles.

The standard of the unified front. However, once you understand the unification thought and the intention of the Unification Church, strange things happen. The teacher tells everyone to go out and evangelize, but those who cannot go out are sneaking away from the teacher, afraid of being seen. No one is saying anything, but they cannot endure it. It is better to go out and evangelize. Isn't that strange? You would feel the same way. 

Also, when students attending school come to the Unification Church and listen to the Word, from then on, after school, they carry their bags and come to church, and when they go home to eat, they digest well. Have you ever felt that? Those who have not felt that are fake.

The connection of the Unification Church is dense. This is because your hearts and bodies like the church and want to be in the church. This is because the church is the place where God's desired words, character, and heart are present. You should not carry God in your hands or in your thoughts, but you must carry Him in your heart. When that happens, you will not be able to do things that go against your heart. The individual unified front must be established based on that standard. But is your heart like that? If it is not, it is fake. It is fake.

Originally, your heart and body must become one. However, that standard has gone awry. From the beginning, the standard of heart does not like to go down. The more it goes up, the more it wants to go up. The more you go up, the closer you get to God. For example, when you save money, you want to save more. People all want to be the president of the world, right? It is the same. Since God's love is the highest, love also tries to rise to the highest.

You must clearly establish this standard of the unified front. If that is not established, it is fake. The will must conquer the heart and the body and lead them. This is the expectation centered on the purpose. This is the philosophy of expectation. There must be a subject that can dominate the heart and body. Therefore, you must communicate with that subject and restart with the purpose in mind. However, this has not been achieved until now. In other words, you have left your position. This is the fall.

You must establish this expectation of the family starting from the family, centered on the husband. When the husband is weak, the wife must take the lead to establish it. When that happens, even if the husband feels bad, he cannot help it. Anyone must become the subject and unite around him to sort things out. Thus, starting from that united family, you must achieve a united tribe, a united nation, and a united world. Then, you must connect with God's love and reach God's heart. You must connect to God's heart bundle. Therefore, when the external standard connects to God's heart, unity unfolds there.

Just as God desires a unified world, humans also desire a unified world, right? It is the same. In that unified world, God becomes the plus, and the world united with God's heart becomes the minus. You must achieve this unified front. If the Unification Church establishes this standard, there is no need for evangelism. There is no need for much evangelism. Because if the individual family, the tribal family, and the national family are resolved—there is a core in the family—then when that standard connects to the world, the world will automatically be restored. Do you know that all 30 million people must be restored?

The path of goodness. Looking at this victorious unified front, you are told to go through the individual, family, tribe, and nation. From this perspective, I have spoken to you about being a tribal messiah. Can one become a tribal messiah without being one with God's love? If one is not one with God's love, one cannot become a messiah. Men and women must be those who stand on that standard to receive blessings and establish families. Just as the Holy Spirit and Jesus become one, resulting in the birth of children of faith, you too must establish a standard of becoming one in reality so that you can reproduce children from a flat position. Only then can you speak of being a tribal messiah. Do you understand?

Therefore, even if it means sacrificing the individual, you must establish the family. Even if the parents must sacrifice, they must save their children. Parents will go down the path of death to save their children. Is it more common for parents to sacrifice for their children or for children to sacrifice for their parents? This is the heavenly law. Parents must save their children. If they do not save their children, the path of the parents will be blocked. And the children of that family need relatives. They must sacrifice for their relatives. Such families are revered and respected as good families in the neighborhood.

When they are revered and respected by those around them, what they give returns to them. Moreover, they become a group that can support them, allowing them to take charge. Is that right? Do you understand? It means that you can make them your allies and harvest the fruits centered around yourself. That is why I am telling you to sacrifice. Therefore, families that sacrifice for their relatives or tribes can harvest all those tribes as their fruits. Because of that, those tribes will all come to that family asking for help. Thus, families must sacrifice for their tribes. And tribes must sacrifice for their nations. It is good for tribes to sacrifice for nations and states. Furthermore, it is good for a nation to sacrifice for the world. That is the normal path of goodness.

Thus, goodness is found after sacrifice. In other words, goodness is harvested after sacrifice. In other words, God's operation is to take and reclaim. Satan's operation is to strike and take away. Historically, looking at the rise and fall of various countries in the world, you can understand this. Those who seize power by killing others and shedding blood ultimately perish. Many nations have perished in this way, as history shows.

From a global standard, bring God into your sphere of life. However, religious people have not perished because they have sacrificed themselves and reclaimed, and instead, they have expanded their influence globally over thousands of years. Historical facts cannot be changed. A good person is one who seeks to sacrifice for others, while an evil person is one who seeks to use others for their own benefit. Such villains perish.

So what does the Unification Church propose? Is it to make the people of the Republic of Korea into servants centered on the Unification Church? No. We are saying that we should serve the Republic of Korea with the heart of parents. Just as parents treat their children, we should serve, teach, and enlighten the nation, establishing that heart as a tradition. When they come to understand, we...
They will realize that they are in the position of parents, so even if you tell them not to follow, they will follow, and even if you tell them not to listen, they will listen to our words. Do you understand? Now, in the 1970s, we must make these principled contents explicit and establish a victorious unification front. Thus, we must unify this and make it manifest. You yourselves must take on that responsibility. You must push yourselves to live in such an environment. Do you understand? "Yes." At the same time, you must work to connect everything with global trends.

Therefore, starting this year, we will hold many Asian or global conferences. In any case, the Unification Church will present many global issues in the future. In order for you to keep pace with that, you must have God fully in your living realm from a global standard. In other words, you should focus on creating co-workers before and after the path you take, to elevate the living stage to heaven. Then, the path you take will absolutely not be lonely. You will surely feel that God is with you in your life. Furthermore, this will leave a foundation on earth for future generations to testify that God is with you. Regarding this issue, we have set the slogan of "Victorious Unification Front" for this year, so please keep this in mind.

<Prayer> Father, as we enter the 1970s, you have presented the tremendous task of the victorious unification front before your beloved children, both those in Korea and those around the world. We understand that this unification front must not be external but internal, starting from our individual victories to become the center of families, and further to become the center of clans, nations, and the world. Thus, we recognize the enormous task of connecting to the path that can directly align with God's original heart standard.

Father, how much effort have you put into the historical process woven around Christianity? How much effort have you made for the Unification Church to lay such a foundation? Thinking of this makes us feel anxious, unable to leave the path we must take even for a moment. Knowing your sorrowful image and form, we lament that we cannot be dutiful children or loyal subjects, and we struggle to think of how we can comfort you.

Allow us to experience that you are not far away, but that you are with us. We earnestly hope and wish for this. In the not-so-distant future, Korea must become your beloved nation of blessing. Looking at the tremendous reality of being divided into North and South, we need to know who can unify the North and South, and how many groups can unite with you.

We know that we do not need to worry about how to form a unification front that can unify North and South Korea, connect Japan and China in Asia, and ultimately push out the Soviet Union and China, as well as how to restore these nations before you. We understand that you are preparing everything for the world, and before we worry, you have worried a thousand or ten thousand times. We must become those who absolutely obey your words and commands.

We earnestly hope and wish to understand how to discover ourselves who can decide to live or die centered on your words and your heart. Now, the path we must take is not only concerning the North but also how to push out China and the Soviet Union and bring Asia back to you. Furthermore, how to bring the world back to you is a great trial that we must fight against in the future, and we must prepare from now on. We must save time from now on. We must not spare any effort needed to walk that path.

In order to meet all the standards you require, we must be able to be grateful for any sacrifices we make. Thus, we must become a group that can establish such families, tribes, and nations. Having passed through the 1960s to lay the foundation for the church, we are now starting towards the 1970s to lay the foundation for the nation and humanity to live, so Father! We earnestly hope and wish for your protection and companionship.

As we reflect on the journey we have walked so far, we have seen this day without dying through trials and pains, and we have set conditions to stand before your will even if we must die. Now, we must step away from all the detours we have taken in the history of the past and, with the sound of the trumpet of heavenly liberation, embrace your heart, becoming sons and daughters who fulfill the duty of filial piety and loyalty. Even if we have nothing left in our bodies, if we can say we would die for that, we will surely know that we have become your sons and daughters.

Now, please protect the path they must take, protect the path the Unification Church must take, protect the path this nation must take, and protect the path the world must take. Thus, we earnestly request that the victorious world of your joy may come quickly, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
